 8796                display: 'flex',
 8797                alignItems: 'center',
 8798                justifyContent: 'space-between',
 8799                p: 1,
 8800                borderRadius: 1,
 8801                backgroundColor: isSelected ? 'action.selected' : 'transparent',
 8802                '&:hover': {
 8803                  backgroundColor: 'action.hover',
 8804                },
 8805                cursor: 'pointer',
 8806              }}
 8807              onClick={() => {
 8808                setSelectedMenu(menu);
 8809                onSelectMenu?.(menu);
 8810              }}
 8811              draggable
 8812              onDragStart={(e) => {
 8813                setDraggedItem(menu);
 8814                e.dataTransfer.effectAllowed = 'move';
 8815              }}
 8816              onDragOver={(e) => {
 8817                e.preventDefault();
 8818                e.dataTransfer.dropEffect = 'move';
 8819              }}
 8820              onDrop={(e) => {
 8821                e.preventDefault();
 8822                if (draggedItem && draggedItem.id !== menu.id) {
 8823                  handleReorder(draggedItem, menu);
 8824                }
 8825              }}
 8826            >
 8827              <Box sx={{ display: 'flex', alignItems: 'center', gap: 1 }}>
 8828                <IconMenu2 size={16} />
 8829                <Typography variant="body2" fontWeight={menu.is_active ? 'medium' : 'normal'}>
 8830                  {menu.label}
 8831                </Typography>
 8832                {!menu.is_active && (
 8833                  <Chip label="Inactive" size="small" color="default" variant="outlined" />
 8834                )}
 8835                {menu.path && (
 8836                  <Typography variant="caption" color="text.secondary" fontFamily="monospace">
 8837                    {menu.path}
 8838                  </Typography>
 8839                )}
 8840              </Box>
 8841              <Box sx={{ display: 'flex', alignItems: 'center', gap: 0.5 }}>
 8842                {menu.roles && menu.roles.length > 0 && (
 8843                  <Chip
 8844                    label={`${menu.roles.length} role${menu.roles.length > 1 ? 's' : ''}`}
 8845                    size="small"
 8846                    variant="outlined"
 8847                    color="info"
 8848                  />
 8849                )}
 8850                <Tooltip title="Add Child">
 8851                  <IconButton
 8852                    size="small"
 8853                    onClick={(e) => {
 8854                      e.stopPropagation();
 8855                      setEditDialog({ open: true, mode: 'create', parentId: menu.id });
 8856                    }}
 8857                  >
 8858                    <IconPlus size={14} />
 8859                  </IconButton>
 8860                </Tooltip>
 8861                <Tooltip title="Edit">
 8862                  <IconButton
 8863                    size="small"
 8864                    onClick={(e) => {
 8865                      e.stopPropagation();
 8866                      setEditDialog({ open: true, mode: 'edit', menu });
 8867                    }}
 8868                  >
 8869                    <IconEdit size={14} />
 8870                  </IconButton>
 8871                </Tooltip>
 8872                <Tooltip title="Delete">
 8873                  <IconButton
 8874                    size="small"
 8875                    onClick={(e) => {
 8876                      e.stopPropagation();
 8877                      handleDelete(menu.id!);
 8878                    }}
 8879                  >
 8880                    <IconTrash size={14} />
 8881                  </IconButton>
 8882                </Tooltip>
 8883              </Box>
 8884            </Box>
 8885          )}
 8886          sx={{
 8887            '& .MuiTree-item': {
 8888              borderRadius: 1,
 8889            },
 8890          }}
 8891        >
 8892          {hasChildren && menu.children!.map(child => renderMenuItem(child))}
 8893        </TreeItem>
 8894      );
 8895    };
 8896    const handleDelete = (id: number) => {
 8897      if (window.confirm('Are you sure you want to delete this menu item?')) {
 8898        deleteMutation.mutate({ id });
 8899      }
 8900    };
 8901    const handleReorder = (draggedItem: MenuNode, targetItem: MenuNode) => {
 8902      // Find all items that need to be updated
 8903      const allItems = flatMenus.filter(item => item.parent_id === targetItem.parent_id);
 8904      // Remove the dragged item from its original position
 8905      const remainingItems = allItems.filter(item => item.id !== draggedItem.id);
 8906      // Insert the dragged item at the target position
 8907      const targetIndex = remainingItems.findIndex(item => item.id === targetItem.id);
 8908      remainingItems.splice(targetIndex, 0, draggedItem);
 8909      // Update order indexes
 8910      const reorderData: ReorderMenuData = {
 8911        items: remainingItems.map((item, index) => ({
 8912          id: item.id!,
 8913          parent_id: item.parent_id,
 8914          order_index: index,
 8915        })),
 8916      };
 8917      // Also update the parent relationship if needed
 8918      if (targetItem.id !== draggedItem.id) {
 8919        reorderData.items.forEach(item => {
 8920          if (item.id === draggedItem.id) {
 8921            item.parent_id = targetItem.parent_id;
 8922          }
 8923        });
 8924      }
 8925      reorderMutation.mutate(reorderData);
 8926    };
 8927    const formatRoles = (roles: string[]) => {
 8928      if (!roles || roles.length === 0) return 'None';
 8929      const roleColors: Record<string, string> = {
 8930        super_admin: 'error',
 8931        admin: 'warning',
 8932        user: 'info',
 8933        guest: 'default',
 8934      };
 8935      return (
 8936        <Box sx={{ display: 'flex', gap: 0.5, flexWrap: 'wrap' }}>
 8937          {roles.map((role) => (
 8938            <Chip
 8939              key={role}
 8940              label={role}
 8941              size="small"
 8942            />
 8943          ))}
 8944        </Box>
 8945      );
 8946    };
 8947    if (error) {
 8948      return (
 8949        <Box sx={{ p: 2 }}>
 8950          <Alert severity="error" sx={{ mb: 2 }}>
 8951            Failed to load menu tree: {(error as Error).message}
 8952          </Alert>
 8953          <Button onClick={() => refetch()} startIcon={<IconRefresh size={16} />}>
 8954            Retry
 8955          </Button>
 8956        </Box>
 8957      );
 8958    }
 8959    return (
 8960      <Box sx={{ height: '100%', display: 'flex', flexDirection: 'column' }}>
 8961        {/* Toolbar */}
 8962        <Box sx={{ p: 2, borderBottom: 1, borderColor: 'divider' }}>
 8963          <Stack direction="row" spacing={1} alignItems="center" justifyContent="space-between">
 8964            <Typography variant="h6" display="flex" alignItems="center" gap={1}>
 8965              <IconMenu2 size={20} />
 8966              Menu Tree
 8967            </Typography>
 8968            <Box sx={{ display: 'flex', gap: 1 }}>
 8969              <Button
 8970                startIcon={<IconPlus size={16} />}
 8971                onClick={() => setEditDialog({ open: true, mode: 'create' })}
 8972                variant="contained"
 8973                size="small"
 8974              >
 8975                Add Root Item
 8976              </Button>
 8977              <Button
 8978                startIcon={<IconRefresh size={16} />}
 8979                onClick={() => refetch()}
 8980                variant="outlined"
 8981                size="small"
 8982              >
 8983                Refresh
 8984              </Button>
 8985            </Box>
 8986          </Stack>
 8987        </Box>
 8988        {/* Tree View */}
 8989        <Box sx={{ flex: 1, overflow: 'auto', p: 1 }}>
 8990          {isLoading ? (
 8991            <Box sx={{ display: 'flex', justifyContent: 'center', p: 4 }}>
 8992              <Typography>Loading menu tree...</Typography>
 8993            </Box>
 8994          ) : (
 8995            <TreeView
 8996              defaultCollapseIcon={<IconChevronDown />}
 8997              defaultExpandIcon={<IconChevronRight />}
 8998              defaultEndIcon={<IconFolder />}
 8999              getItemId={(item) => String(item.id)} // Custom ID getter for normalized items
 9000              sx={{ height: '100%', flexGrow: 1 }}
 9001            >
 9002              {normalizedMenuTree.map(renderMenuItem)}
 9003            </TreeView>
 9004          )}
 9005        </Box>
 9006        {/* Details Panel */}
 9007        {selectedMenu && (
 9008          <Paper elevation={3} sx={{ p: 2, mt: 2 }}>
 9009            <Typography variant="h6" gutterBottom>
 9010              Menu Details
 9011            </Typography>
 9012            <Stack spacing={2}>
 9013              <Box>
 9014                <Typography variant="subtitle2" color="text.secondary">
 9015                  Label
 9016                </Typography>
 9017                <Typography>{selectedMenu.label}</Typography>
 9018              </Box>
 9019              <Box>
 9020                <Typography variant="subtitle2" color="text.secondary">
 9021                  Key Name
 9022                </Typography>
 9023                <Typography fontFamily="monospace">{selectedMenu.key_name}</Typography>
 9024              </Box>
 9025              {selectedMenu.path && (
 9026                <Box>
 9027                  <Typography variant="subtitle2" color="text.secondary">
 9028                    Target Path
 9029                  </Typography>
 9030                  <Typography fontFamily="monospace">{selectedMenu.path}</Typography>
 9031                </Box>
 9032              )}
 9033              <Box>
 9034                <Typography variant="subtitle2" color="text.secondary">
 9035                  Roles Required
 9036                </Typography>
 9037                {formatRoles(selectedMenu.roles)}
 9038              </Box>
 9039              <Box>
 9040                <Typography variant="subtitle2" color="text.secondary">
 9041                  Status
 9042                </Typography>
 9043                <Chip
 9044                  label={selectedMenu.is_active ? 'Active' : 'Inactive'}
 9045                  color={selectedMenu.is_active ? 'success' : 'default'}
 9046                  size="small"
 9047                />
 9048              </Box>
 9049              <Box>
 9050                <Typography variant="subtitle2" color="text.secondary">
 9051                  Order Index
 9052                </Typography>
 9053                <Typography>{selectedMenu.order_index}</Typography>
 9054              </Box>
 9055              <Box>
 9056                <Typography variant="subtitle2" color="text.secondary">
 9057                  Last Updated
 9058                </Typography>
 9059                <Typography variant="caption">
 9060                  {new Date(selectedMenu.updated_at).toLocaleString()}
 9061                </Typography>
 9062              </Box>
 9063            </Stack>
 9064          </Paper>
 9065        )}
 9066        {/* Edit Dialog */}
 9067        <MenuEditDialog
 9068          open={editDialog.open}
 9069          mode={editDialog.mode}
 9070          menu={editDialog.menu}
 9071          parentId={editDialog.parentId}
 9072          onSubmit={(data) => {
 9073            if (editDialog.mode === 'create') {
 9074              createMutation.mutate(data as CreateMenuData);
 9075            } else if (editDialog.menu) {
 9076              updateMutation.mutate({ id: editDialog.menu.id, data });
 9077            }
 9078          }}
 9079          onClose={() => setEditDialog({ open: false, mode: 'create' })}
 9080          isLoading={createMutation.isPending || updateMutation.isPending}
 9081          availableParents={flatMenus.filter(m => !m.parent_id && (!editDialog.menu || m.id !== editDialog.menu.id))}
 9082        />
 9083      </Box>
 9084    );
 9085  };
 9086  interface MenuEditDialogProps {
 9087    open: boolean;
 9088    mode: 'create' | 'edit';
 9089    menu?: MenuNode;
 9090    parentId?: number;
 9091    onSubmit: (data: CreateMenuData | UpdateMenuData) => void;
 9092    onClose: () => void;
 9093    isLoading?: boolean;
 9094    availableParents: MenuNode[];
 9095  }
 9096  const MenuEditDialog: React.FC<MenuEditDialogProps> = ({
 9097    open,
 9098    mode,
 9099    menu,
 9100    parentId,
 9101    onSubmit,
 9102    onClose,
 9103    isLoading,
 9104    availableParents,
 9105  }) => {
 9106    const [formData, setFormData] = useState({
 9107      parent_id: parentId || null,
 9108      key_name: '',
 9109      label: '',
 9110      icon: '',
 9111      path: '',
 9112      roles: ['user'],
 9113      is_active: true,
 9114      order_index: 0,
 9115    });
 9116    React.useEffect(() => {
 9117      if (menu) {
 9118        setFormData({
 9119          parent_id: menu.parent_id || null,
 9120          key_name: menu.key_name,
 9121          label: menu.label,
 9122          icon: menu.icon || '',
 9123          path: menu.path || '',
 9124          roles: menu.roles,
 9125          is_active: menu.is_active,
 9126          order_index: menu.order_index,
 9127        });
 9128      } else {
 9129        setFormData({
 9130          parent_id: parentId || null,
 9131          key_name: '',
 9132          label: '',
 9133          icon: '',
 9134          path: '',
 9135          roles: ['user'],
 9136          is_active: true,
 9137          order_index: 0,
 9138        });
 9139      }
 9140    }, [menu, parentId, open]);
 9141    const handleSubmit = (e: React.FormEvent) => {
 9142      e.preventDefault();
 9143      onSubmit(formData);
 9144    };
 9145    const handleAddRole = () => {
 9146      const newRole = prompt('Enter role name:');
 9147      if (newRole && !formData.roles.includes(newRole)) {
 9148        setFormData(prev => ({
 9149          ...prev,
 9150          roles: [...prev.roles, newRole]
 9151        }));
 9152      }
 9153    };
 9154    const handleRemoveRole = (roleToRemove: string) => {
 9155      setFormData(prev => ({
 9156        ...prev,
 9157        roles: prev.roles.filter(role => role !== roleToRemove)
 9158      }));
 9159    };
 9160    return (
 9161      <Dialog open={open} onClose={onClose} maxWidth="md" fullWidth>
 9162        <form onSubmit={handleSubmit}>
 9163          <DialogTitle>
 9164            {mode === 'create' ? 'Create Menu Item' : 'Edit Menu Item'}
 9165          </DialogTitle>
 9166          <DialogContent>
 9167            <Stack spacing={3} sx={{ mt: 1 }}>
 9168              <TextField
 9169                required
 9170                fullWidth
 9171                label="Label"
 9172                value={formData.label}
 9173                onChange={(e) => setFormData(prev => ({ ...prev, label: e.target.value }))}
 9174                placeholder="Menu item label"
 9175              />
 9176              <TextField
 9177                required
 9178                fullWidth
 9179                label="Key Name"
 9180                value={formData.key_name}
 9181                onChange={(e) => setFormData(prev => ({ ...prev, key_name: e.target.value }))}
 9182                placeholder="unique-key-name"
 9183                helperText="Unique key for this menu item (used internally)"
 9184              />
 9185              <TextField
 9186                fullWidth
 9187                label="Icon"
 9188                value={formData.icon}
 9189                onChange={(e) => setFormData(prev => ({ ...prev, icon: e.target.value }))}
 9190                placeholder="IconName"
 9191                helperText="Icon name (from icon library)"
 9192              />
 9193              <TextField
 9194                fullWidth
 9195                label="Path"
 9196                value={formData.path}
 9197                onChange={(e) => setFormData(prev => ({ ...prev, path: e.target.value }))}
 9198                placeholder="/target/path"
 9199                helperText="Target route path (optional)"
 9200              />
 9201              <FormControl fullWidth>
 9202                <InputLabel>Parent Menu</InputLabel>
 9203                <Select
 9204                  value={formData.parent_id || ''}
 9205                  onChange={(e) => setFormData(prev => ({ ...prev, parent_id: e.target.value || null }))}
 9206                  label="Parent Menu"
 9207                >
 9208                  <MenuItem value="">Root Level</MenuItem>
 9209                  {availableParents.map((parent) => (
 9210                    <MenuItem key={parent.id} value={parent.id}>
 9211                      {parent.label}
 9212                    </MenuItem>
 9213                  ))}
 9214                </Select>
 9215              </FormControl>
 9216              <Box>
 9217                <Typography variant="subtitle2" gutterBottom>
 9218                  Roles Required
 9219                </Typography>
 9220                <Box sx={{ display: 'flex', gap: 1, flexWrap: 'wrap', mb: 1 }}>
 9221                  {formData.roles.map((role) => (
 9222                    <Chip
 9223                      key={role}
 9224                      label={role}
 9225                      onDelete={() => handleRemoveRole(role)}
 9226                      size="small"
 9227                    />
 9228                  ))}
 9229                </Box>
 9230                <Button
 9231                  size="small"
 9232                  onClick={handleAddRole}
 9233                  startIcon={<IconPlus size={14} />}
 9234                >
 9235                  Add Role
 9236                </Button>
 9237              </Box>
 9238              <Stack direction="row" spacing={3}>
 9239                <TextField
 9240                  type="number"
 9241                  label="Order Index"
 9242                  value={formData.order_index}
 9243                  onChange={(e) => setFormData(prev => ({ ...prev, order_index: parseInt(e.target.value) || 0 }))}
 9244                  inputProps={{ min: 0 }}
 9245                  sx={{ width: 150 }}
 9246                />
 9247                <FormControlLabel
 9248                  control={
 9249                    <Switch
 9250                      checked={formData.is_active}
 9251                      onChange={(e) => setFormData(prev => ({ ...prev, is_active: e.target.checked }))}
 9252                    />
 9253                  }
 9254                  label="Active"
 9255                />
 9256              </Stack>
 9257            </Stack>
 9258          </DialogContent>
 9259          <DialogActions>
 9260            <Button onClick={onClose} disabled={isLoading}>
 9261              <IconX size={16} style={{ marginRight: 8 }} />
 9262              Cancel
 9263            </Button>
 9264            <Button
 9265              type="submit"
 9266              variant="contained"
 9267              disabled={isLoading}
 9268              startIcon={<IconCheck size={16} />}
 9269            >
 9270              {isLoading ? 'Saving...' : (mode === 'create' ? 'Create' : 'Update')}
 9271            </Button>
 9272          </DialogActions>
 9273        </form>
 9274      </Dialog>
 9275    );
 9276  };
 9277  export default MenuTree;

 9283  /**
 9284   * Tree Inspector Component
 9285   * Development tool for inspecting tree item IDs and paths to diagnose conflicts
 9286   */
 9287  import React, { useState, useMemo } from 'react';
 9288  import {
 9289    Box,
 9290    Paper,
 9291    Typography,
 9292    Button,
 9293    Stack,
 9294    Table,
 9295    TableBody,
 9296    TableCell,
 9297    TableContainer,
 9298    TableHead,
 9299    TableRow,
 9300    Chip,
 9301    IconButton,
 9302    Collapse,
 9303    TextField,
 9304    Alert,
 9305    Divider,
 9306  } from '@mui/material';
 9307  import {
 9308    IconTree,
 9309    IconRefresh,
 9310    IconChevronDown,
 9311    IconChevronRight,
 9312    IconSearch,
 9313    IconAlertTriangle,
 9314    IconCopy,
 9315  } from '@tabler/icons-react';
 9316  import { useQuery } from '@tanstack/react-query';
 9317  import { routerMenuStudioAPI } from '../router-menu-studio/api';
 9318  import { normalizeTreeItems, validateTreeItems } from '../router-menu-studio/normalizeTreeItems';
 9319  import { toast } from 'react-hot-toast';
 9320  interface TreeItem {
 9321    id: string | number;
 9322    label?: string;
 9323    key_name?: string;
 9324    path?: string;
 9325    computedId?: string;
 9326    computedPath?: string;
 9327    level: number;
 9328    children?: TreeItem[];
 9329    originalId?: string | number;
 9330    hasConflict?: boolean;
 9331  }
 9332  const TreeInspector: React.FC = () => {
 9333    const [expandedRows, setExpandedRows] = useState<Set<string>>(new Set());
 9334    const [searchTerm, setSearchTerm] = useState('');
 9335    
 9336    // Fetch menu tree data
 9337    const { data: menuTree = [], isLoading, error, refetch } = useQuery({
 9338      queryKey: ['menu-tree-inspector'],
 9339      queryFn: () => routerMenuStudioAPI.getMenuTree(),
 9340    });
 9341    // Process tree items to extract inspection data
 9342    const inspectionData = useMemo(() => {
 9343      if (!menuTree?.length) return { items: [], conflicts: [], stats: {} };
 9344      // First, normalize the tree to get computed IDs
 9345      const normalizedTree = normalizeTreeItems(menuTree);
 9346      
 9347      // Flatten tree into inspection items
 9348      const flattenTree = (items: any[], level = 0, parentPath = ''): TreeItem[] => {
 9349        const result: TreeItem[] = [];
 9350        
 9351        items.forEach((item, index) => {
 9352          const computedPath = parentPath ? `${parentPath}[${index}]` : `root[${index}]`;
 9353          const inspectionItem: TreeItem = {
 9354            id: item.id,
 9355            originalId: menuTree.find(orig => orig.id === item.id)?.id,
 9356            label: item.label,
 9357            key_name: item.key_name,
 9358            path: item.path,
 9359            computedId: String(item.id),
 9360            computedPath,
 9361            level,
 9362            children: item.children ? flattenTree(item.children, level + 1, computedPath) : undefined,
 9363          };
 9364          
 9365          result.push(inspectionItem);
 9366          
 9367          if (item.children?.length) {
 9368            result.push(...flattenTree(item.children, level + 1, computedPath));
 9369          }
 9370        });
 9371        
 9372        return result;
 9373      };
 9374      const allItems = flattenTree(normalizedTree);
 9375      
 9376      // Find conflicts (duplicate computed IDs)
 9377      const idCounts = new Map<string, number>();
 9378      allItems.forEach(item => {
 9379        const count = idCounts.get(item.computedId!) || 0;
 9380        idCounts.set(item.computedId!, count + 1);
 9381      });
 9382      
 9383      const conflicts = Array.from(idCounts.entries())
 9384        .filter(([, count]) => count > 1)
 9385        .map(([id]) => id);
 9386      
 9387      // Mark conflicted items
 9388      allItems.forEach(item => {
 9389        item.hasConflict = conflicts.includes(item.computedId!);
 9390      });
 9391      
 9392      // Calculate stats
 9393      const stats = {
 9394        totalItems: allItems.length,
 9395        conflicts: conflicts.length,
 9396        maxDepth: Math.max(...allItems.map(item => item.level), 0),
 9397        itemsWithPaths: allItems.filter(item => item.path).length,
 9398        itemsWithKeys: allItems.filter(item => item.key_name).length,
 9399      };
 9400      return { items: allItems, conflicts, stats };
 9401    }, [menuTree]);
 9402    // Filter items based on search term
 9403    const filteredItems = useMemo(() => {
 9404      if (!searchTerm) return inspectionData.items;
 9405      
 9406      const term = searchTerm.toLowerCase();
 9407      return inspectionData.items.filter(item =>
 9408        item.label?.toLowerCase().includes(term) ||
 9409        item.key_name?.toLowerCase().includes(term) ||
 9410        item.path?.toLowerCase().includes(term) ||
 9411        item.computedId?.toLowerCase().includes(term) ||
 9412        item.computedPath?.toLowerCase().includes(term)
 9413      );
 9414    }, [inspectionData.items, searchTerm]);
 9415    const toggleRowExpansion = (itemId: string) => {
 9416      const newExpanded = new Set(expandedRows);
 9417      if (newExpanded.has(itemId)) {
 9418        newExpanded.delete(itemId);
 9419      } else {
 9420        newExpanded.add(itemId);
 9421      }
 9422      setExpandedRows(newExpanded);
 9423    };
 9424    const copyToClipboard = (text: string) => {
 9425      navigator.clipboard.writeText(text).then(() => {
 9426        toast.success('Copied to clipboard');
 9427      });
 9428    };
 9429    const renderItemRow = (item: TreeItem) => {
 9430      const hasChildren = item.children && item.children.length > 0;
 9431      const isExpanded = expandedRows.has(item.computedId!);
 9432      const indentLevel = item.level * 20;
 9433      return (
 9434        <React.Fragment key={item.computedId}>
 9435          <TableRow 
 9436            sx={{ 
 9437              backgroundColor: item.hasConflict ? 'error.light' : 'transparent',
 9438              '&:hover': { backgroundColor: 'action.hover' }
 9439            }}
 9440          >
 9441            <TableCell sx={{ pl: `${12 + indentLevel}px` }}>
 9442              <Box sx={{ display: 'flex', alignItems: 'center', gap: 1 }}>
 9443                {hasChildren ? (
 9444                  <IconButton
 9445                    size="small"
 9446                    onClick={() => toggleRowExpansion(item.computedId!)}
 9447                  >
 9448                    {isExpanded ? <IconChevronDown size={16} /> : <IconChevronRight size={16} />}
 9449                  </IconButton>
 9450                ) : (
 9451                  <Box sx={{ width: 32 }} />
 9452                )}
 9453                
 9454                <Typography variant="body2" fontWeight="medium">
 9455                  {item.label || '(no label)'}
 9456                </Typography>
 9457                
 9458                {item.hasConflict && (
 9459                  <Chip 
 9460                    label="CONFLICT" 
 9461                    size="small" 
 9462                    color="error" 
 9463                    variant="outlined"
 9464                    icon={<IconAlertTriangle size={12} />}
 9465                  />
 9466                )}
 9467              </Box>
 9468            </TableCell>
 9469            
 9470            <TableCell>
 9471              <Box sx={{ display: 'flex', alignItems: 'center', gap: 1 }}>
 9472                <Typography variant="caption" fontFamily="monospace">
 9473                  {item.computedId}
 9474                </Typography>
 9475                <IconButton 
 9476                  size="small" 
 9477                  onClick={() => copyToClipboard(item.computedId!)}
 9478                >
 9479                  <IconCopy size={12} />
 9480                </IconButton>
 9481              </Box>
 9482            </TableCell>
 9483            
 9484            <TableCell>
 9485              <Typography variant="caption" color="text.secondary">
 9486                {item.computedPath}
 9487              </Typography>
 9488            </TableCell>
 9489            
 9490            <TableCell>
 9491              <Typography variant="caption" fontFamily="monospace">
 9492                {item.key_name || '-'}
 9493              </Typography>
 9494            </TableCell>
 9495            
 9496            <TableCell>
 9497              <Typography variant="caption" fontFamily="monospace">
 9498                {item.path || '-'}
 9499              </Typography>
 9500            </TableCell>
 9501            
 9502            <TableCell>
 9503              <Typography variant="caption">
 9504                {item.originalId}
 9505              </Typography>
 9506            </TableCell>
 9507          </TableRow>
 9508          
 9509          {hasChildren && isExpanded && (
 9510            <TableRow>
 9511              <TableCell colSpan={6} sx={{ p: 0, border: 'none' }}>
 9512                <Collapse in={isExpanded}>
 9513                  <Box sx={{ p: 1 }}>
 9514                    {/* Child items will be rendered by the main loop */}
 9515                  </Box>
 9516                </Collapse>
 9517              </TableCell>
 9518            </TableRow>
 9519          )}
 9520        </React.Fragment>
 9521      );
 9522    };
 9523    if (error) {
 9524      return (
 9525        <Box sx={{ p: 3 }}>
 9526          <Alert severity="error" sx={{ mb: 2 }}>
 9527            Failed to load menu tree data: {(error as Error).message}
 9528          </Alert>
 9529          <Button onClick={() => refetch()} startIcon={<IconRefresh size={16} />}>
 9530            Retry
 9531          </Button>
 9532        </Box>
 9533      );
 9534    }
 9535    return (
 9536      <Box sx={{ p: 3 }}>
 9537        {/* Header */}
 9538        <Stack direction="row" spacing={2} alignItems="center" sx={{ mb: 3 }}>
 9539          <IconTree size={24} />
 9540          <Typography variant="h5">Tree Inspector</Typography>
 9541          <Button
 9542            startIcon={<IconRefresh size={16} />}
 9543            onClick={() => refetch()}
 9544            variant="outlined"
 9545            size="small"
 9546          >
 9547            Refresh
 9548          </Button>
 9549        </Stack>
 9550        <Typography variant="body2" color="text.secondary" sx={{ mb: 3 }}>
 9551          Development tool for inspecting tree item IDs and paths to diagnose conflicts.
 9552          This panel shows the computed IDs that will be used by the TreeView component.
 9553        </Typography>
 9554        {/* Stats Panel */}
 9555        <Paper variant="outlined" sx={{ p: 2, mb: 3 }}>
 9556          <Typography variant="h6" gutterBottom>
 9557            Statistics
 9558          </Typography>
 9559          <Stack direction="row" spacing={3}>
 9560            <Box>
 9561              <Typography variant="caption" color="text.secondary">
 9562                Total Items
 9563              </Typography>
 9564              <Typography variant="h6">
 9565                {inspectionData.stats.totalItems}
 9566              </Typography>
 9567            </Box>
 9568            <Box>
 9569              <Typography variant="caption" color="text.secondary">
 9570                ID Conflicts
 9571              </Typography>
 9572              <Typography variant="h6" color={inspectionData.stats.conflicts > 0 ? 'error.main' : 'success.main'}>
 9573                {inspectionData.stats.conflicts}
 9574              </Typography>
 9575            </Box>
 9576            <Box>
 9577              <Typography variant="caption" color="text.secondary">
 9578                Max Depth
 9579              </Typography>
 9580              <Typography variant="h6">
 9581                {inspectionData.stats.maxDepth}
 9582              </Typography>
 9583            </Box>
 9584            <Box>
 9585              <Typography variant="caption" color="text.secondary">
 9586                Items with Paths
 9587              </Typography>
 9588              <Typography variant="h6">
 9589                {inspectionData.stats.itemsWithPaths}
 9590              </Typography>
 9591            </Box>
 9592            <Box>
 9593              <Typography variant="caption" color="text.secondary">
 9594                Items with Keys
 9595              </Typography>
 9596              <Typography variant="h6">
 9597                {inspectionData.stats.itemsWithKeys}
 9598              </Typography>
 9599            </Box>
 9600          </Stack>
 9601        </Paper>
 9602        {/* Conflicts Alert */}
 9603        {inspectionData.conflicts.length > 0 && (
 9604          <Alert severity="warning" sx={{ mb: 3 }}>
 9605            <Typography variant="subtitle2" gutterBottom>
 9606              ID Conflicts Detected
 9607            </Typography>
 9608            <Typography variant="body2">
 9609              The following computed IDs appear multiple times: {inspectionData.conflicts.join(', ')}
 9610            </Typography>
 9611          </Alert>
 9612        )}
 9613        {/* Search */}
 9614        <Box sx={{ mb: 3 }}>
 9615          <TextField
 9616            fullWidth
 9617            size="small"
 9618            placeholder="Search by label, key, path, or computed ID..."
 9619            value={searchTerm}
 9620            onChange={(e) => setSearchTerm(e.target.value)}
 9621            InputProps={{
 9622              startAdornment: <IconSearch size={16} style={{ marginRight: 8, color: '#666' }} />,
 9623            }}
 9624          />
 9625        </Box>
 9626        {/* Tree Table */}
 9627        <TableContainer component={Paper} variant="outlined">
 9628          <Table size="small" stickyHeader>
 9629            <TableHead>
 9630              <TableRow>
 9631                <TableCell>Label</TableCell>
 9632                <TableCell>Computed ID</TableCell>
 9633                <TableCell>Path</TableCell>
 9634                <TableCell>Key Name</TableCell>
 9635                <TableCell>Target Path</TableCell>
 9636                <TableCell>Original ID</TableCell>
 9637              </TableRow>
 9638            </TableHead>
 9639            <TableBody>
 9640              {isLoading ? (
 9641                <TableRow>
 9642                  <TableCell colSpan={6} align="center" sx={{ py: 4 }}>
 9643                    <Typography>Loading tree data...</Typography>
 9644                  </TableCell>
 9645                </TableRow>
 9646              ) : filteredItems.length === 0 ? (
 9647                <TableRow>
 9648                  <TableCell colSpan={6} align="center" sx={{ py: 4 }}>
 9649                    <Typography color="text.secondary">
 9650                      {searchTerm ? 'No items match your search' : 'No tree items found'}
 9651                    </Typography>
 9652                  </TableCell>
 9653                </TableRow>
 9654              ) : (
 9655                filteredItems.map(renderItemRow)
 9656              )}
 9657            </TableBody>
 9658          </Table>
 9659        </TableContainer>
 9660      </Box>
 9661    );
 9662  };
 9663  export default TreeInspector;
 9664  EOF

10255  const fs = require('fs').promises;
10256  const path = require('path');
10257  class BackupCleanup {
10258    constructor(baseDir = '/var/www/orthodoxmetrics/prod') {
10259      this.baseDir = baseDir;
10260    }
10261    async run(mode = 'dry-run') {
10262      const timestamp = new Date().toISOString();
10263      
10264      console.log(`Running backup cleanup in ${mode} mode...`);
10265      // Read legacy reports
10266      const legacyApi = await this.readLegacyApiReport();
10267      const legacyUi = await this.readLegacyUiReport();
10268      // Analyze what needs to be cleaned up
10269      const filesToDelete = await this.identifyFilesToDelete(legacyApi, legacyUi);
10270      const routesToUpdate = await this.identifyRoutesToUpdate(legacyUi);
10271      let bytesFreed = 0;
10272      let filesDeleted = 0;
10273      let routesUpdated = 0;
10274      if (mode === 'apply') {
10275        // Delete legacy files
10276        for (const filePath of filesToDelete) {
10277          try {
10278            const stats = await fs.stat(filePath);
10279            bytesFreed += stats.size;
10280            await fs.unlink(filePath);
10281            filesDeleted++;
10282            console.log(`Deleted: ${filePath}`);
10283          } catch (error) {
10284            console.warn(`Could not delete ${filePath}:`, error.message);
10285          }
10286        }
10287        routesUpdated = routesToUpdate.length;
10288        console.log(`Routes to update: ${routesToUpdate.join(', ')}`);
10289        
10290        await this.addLegacyApiResponses(legacyApi);
10291        
10292      } else {
10293        // Dry run - calculate what would be freed
10294        for (const filePath of filesToDelete) {
10295          try {
10296            const stats = await fs.stat(filePath);
10297            bytesFreed += stats.size;
10298            filesDeleted++;
10299          } catch (error) {
10300            console.warn(`Could not stat ${filePath}:`, error.message);
10301          }
10302        }
10303        routesUpdated = routesToUpdate.length;
10304      }
10305      const report = {
10306        timestamp,
10307        mode,
10308        legacy_api: legacyApi,
10309        legacy_ui: legacyUi,
10310        files_to_delete: filesToDelete,
10311        routes_to_update: routesToUpdate,
10312        summary: {
10313          files_deleted: filesDeleted,
10314          routes_updated: routesUpdated,
10315          bytes_freed: bytesFreed
10316        }
10317      };
10318      // Write cleanup log
10319      const logPath = path.join(
10320        this.baseDir,
10321        'server/src/modules/backup',
10322        `.cleanup-log-${timestamp.replace(/[:.]/g, '-')}.json`
10323      );
10324      await fs.writeFile(logPath, JSON.stringify(report, null, 2));
10325      console.log('\nCleanup Summary:');
10326      console.log(`Mode: ${mode}`);
10327      console.log(`Files ${mode === 'apply' ? 'deleted' : 'to delete'}: ${filesDeleted}`);
10328      console.log(`Routes ${mode === 'apply' ? 'updated' : 'to update'}: ${routesUpdated}`);
10329      console.log(`Bytes ${mode === 'apply' ? 'freed' : 'to free'}: ${bytesFreed}`);
10330      console.log(`Report saved to: ${logPath}`);
10331      return report;
10332    }
10333    async readLegacyApiReport() {
10334      try {
10335        const reportPath = path.join(this.baseDir, 'server/src/modules/backup/.legacy-report.json');
10336        const content = await fs.readFile(reportPath, 'utf8');
10337        const report = JSON.parse(content);
10338        return report.legacy_api_found || [];
10339      } catch (error) {
10340        console.warn('Could not read legacy API report:', error.message);
10341        return [];
10342      }
10343    }
10344    async readLegacyUiReport() {
10345      try {
10346        const reportPath = path.join(this.baseDir, 'features/devel-tools/backup/.legacy-ui-report.json');
10347        const content = await fs.readFile(reportPath, 'utf8');
10348        const report = JSON.parse(content);
10349        return report.legacy_ui_found || [];
10350      } catch (error) {
10351        console.warn('Could not read legacy UI report:', error.message);
10352        return [];
10353      }
10354    }
10355    async identifyFilesToDelete(legacyApi, legacyUi) {
10356      const filesToDelete = [];
10357      // Add legacy API files
10358      for (const api of legacyApi) {
10359        const fullPath = path.join(this.baseDir, api.path);
10360        if (await this.fileExists(fullPath)) {
10361          filesToDelete.push(fullPath);
10362        }
10363      }
10364      // Add legacy UI files
10365      for (const ui of legacyUi) {
10366        const fullPath = path.join(this.baseDir, ui.path);
10367        if (await this.fileExists(fullPath)) {
10368          filesToDelete.push(fullPath);
10369        }
10370      }
10371      return filesToDelete;
10372    }
10373    async identifyRoutesToUpdate(legacyUi) {
10374      const routesToUpdate = [];
10375      const routerFiles = await this.findRouterFiles();
10376      
10377      for (const routerFile of routerFiles) {
10378        try {
10379          const content = await fs.readFile(routerFile, 'utf8');
10380          
10381          for (const ui of legacyUi) {
10382            const componentName = ui.component;
10383            if (content.includes(componentName)) {
10384              if (!routesToUpdate.includes(routerFile)) {
10385                routesToUpdate.push(routerFile);
10386              }
10387            }
10388          }
10389        } catch (error) {
10390          console.warn(`Could not read router file ${routerFile}:`, error.message);
10391        }
10392      }
10393      return routesToUpdate;
10394    }
10395    async findRouterFiles() {
10396      const routerFiles = [];
10397      const searchPaths = [
10398        'front-end/Router.tsx',
10399        'front-end/src/routes/Router.tsx',
10400        'MenuItems.ts',
10401        'front-end/src/layouts/full/vertical/sidebar/MenuItems.ts'
10402      ];
10403      for (const searchPath of searchPaths) {
10404        const fullPath = path.join(this.baseDir, searchPath);
10405        if (await this.fileExists(fullPath)) {
10406          routerFiles.push(fullPath);
10407        }
10408      }
10409      return routerFiles;
10410    }
10411    async addLegacyApiResponses(legacyApi) {
10412      if (legacyApi.length === 0) return;
10413      const legacyRouterPath = path.join(this.baseDir, 'server/src/modules/backup/legacy-api-responses.js');
10414      
10415      const legacyResponseCode = \`
10416  // Legacy backup API - returns 410 Gone
10417  const express = require('express');
10418  const router = express.Router();
10419  // All legacy backup endpoints return 410 Gone
10420  router.all('*', (req, res) => {
10421    res.status(410).json({
10422      success: false,
10423      error: 'Legacy backup API removed',
10424      message: 'This backup API has been replaced. Use /api/backup/* endpoints instead.',
10425      new_endpoint: req.originalUrl.replace('/api/backup-legacy', '/api/backup'),
10426      migration_guide: 'See server/src/modules/backup/README.md for migration instructions'
10427    });
10428  });
10429  module.exports = router;
10430  \`;
10431      await fs.writeFile(legacyRouterPath, legacyResponseCode);
10432      console.log(\`Created legacy API responses at: \${legacyRouterPath}\`);
10433    }
10434    async fileExists(filePath) {
10435      try {
10436        await fs.access(filePath);
10437        return true;
10438      } catch {
10439        return false;
10440      }
10441    }
10442  }
10443  // CLI interface
10444  if (require.main === module) {
10445    const cleanup = new BackupCleanup();
10446    const mode = process.argv[2] === 'apply' ? 'apply' : 'dry-run';
10447    
10448    cleanup.run(mode)
10449      .then(report => {
10450        console.log('\nCleanup completed successfully');
10451        process.exit(0);
10452      })
10453      .catch(error => {
10454        console.error('Cleanup failed:', error);
10455        process.exit(1);
10456      });
10457  }

10461  cd /var/www/orthodoxmetrics/prod && echo 'const fs = require("fs").promises;
10462  const path = require("path");
10463  class BackupCleanup {
10464    constructor(baseDir = "/var/www/orthodoxmetrics/prod") {
10465      this.baseDir = baseDir;
10466    }
10467    async run(mode = "dry-run") {
10468      console.log(`Running backup cleanup in ${mode} mode...`);
10469      // Read legacy reports
10470      const legacyApi = await this.readLegacyApiReport();
10471      const legacyUi = await this.readLegacyUiReport();
10472      console.log("Legacy API found:", legacyApi.length);
10473      console.log("Legacy UI found:", legacyUi.length);
10474      // Identify files to clean up
10475      const filesToDelete = await this.identifyFilesToDelete(legacyApi, legacyUi);
10476      console.log("Files to clean up:", filesToDelete.length);
10477      let bytesFreed = 0;
10478      for (const filePath of filesToDelete) {
10479        try {
10480          const stats = await fs.stat(filePath);
10481          bytesFreed += stats.size;
10482          console.log(`Would delete: ${filePath} (${stats.size} bytes)`);
10483        } catch (error) {
10484          console.warn(`Could not stat ${filePath}:`, error.message);
10485        }
10486      }
10487      console.log(`Total bytes that would be freed: ${bytesFreed}`);
10488      return { filesToDelete, bytesFreed };
10489    }
10490    async readLegacyApiReport() {
10491      try {
10492        const reportPath = path.join(this.baseDir, "server/src/modules/backup/.legacy-report.json");
10493        const content = await fs.readFile(reportPath, "utf8");
10494        const report = JSON.parse(content);
10495        return report.legacy_api_found || [];
10496      } catch (error) {
10497        console.warn("Could not read legacy API report:", error.message);
10498        return [];
10499      }
10500    }
10501    async readLegacyUiReport() {
10502      try {
10503        const reportPath = path.join(this.baseDir, "features/devel-tools/backup/.legacy-ui-report.json");
10504        const content = await fs.readFile(reportPath, "utf8");
10505        const report = JSON.parse(content);
10506        return report.legacy_ui_found || [];
10507      } catch (error) {
10508        console.warn("Could not read legacy UI report:", error.message);
10509        return [];
10510      }
10511    }
10512    async identifyFilesToDelete(legacyApi, legacyUi) {
10513      const filesToDelete = [];
10514      for (const api of legacyApi) {
10515        const fullPath = path.join(this.baseDir, api.path);
10516        if (await this.fileExists(fullPath)) {
10517          filesToDelete.push(fullPath);
10518        }
10519      }
10520      for (const ui of legacyUi) {
10521        const fullPath = path.join(this.baseDir, ui.path);
10522        if (await this.fileExists(fullPath)) {
10523          filesToDelete.push(fullPath);
10524        }
10525      }
10526      return filesToDelete;
10527    }
10528    async fileExists(filePath) {
10529      try {
10530        await fs.access(filePath);
10531        return true;
10532      } catch {
10533        return false;
10534      }
10535    }
10536  }
10537  if (require.main === module) {
10538    const cleanup = new BackupCleanup();
10539    cleanup.run("dry-run").then(() => console.log("Done")).catch(console.error);
10540  }

10583  cd /var/www/orthodoxmetrics/prod && cat > server/src/modules/backup/README.md << 'EOF'
10584  # OrthodoxMetrics Advanced Backup & Restore System
10585  A comprehensive backup and restore system for OrthodoxMetrics that supports file backups, database backups, filtering, diff generation, and safe restoration.
10586  ## Features
10587  - **File Backups**: Tar.gz archives with regex filtering
10588  - **Database Backups**: MySQL dumps with compression
10589  - **Manifests**: JSON and text manifests for each backup
10590  - **Git Index**: Version control for manifests with tagging
10591  - **Diff Generation**: Compare backups without extracting archives
10592  - **Safe Restoration**: Restore to separate locations by default
10593  - **SSE Streaming**: Real-time progress updates
10594  - **Super Admin Only**: Secured with role-based access control
10595  ## API Endpoints
10596  ### Authentication
10597  All endpoints require `super_admin` role.
10598  ### Backup Management
10599  #### `GET /api/backup/recent?limit=50`
10600  Get recent backup jobs and artifacts.
10601  ```bash
10602  curl -H "Authorization: Bearer <TOKEN>" \
10603    "https://orthodoxmetrics.com/api/backup/recent?limit=20"
10604  ```
10605  #### `POST /api/backup/run`
10606  Run a new backup.
10607  ```bash
10608  # Files backup
10609  curl -H "Authorization: Bearer <TOKEN>" \
10610    -H "Content-Type: application/json" \
10611    -X POST "https://orthodoxmetrics.com/api/backup/run" \
10612    -d '{"kind":"files"}'
10613  # Database backup
10614  curl -H "Authorization: Bearer <TOKEN>" \
10615    -H "Content-Type: application/json" \
10616    -X POST "https://orthodoxmetrics.com/api/backup/run" \
10617    -d '{"kind":"db"}'
10618  # Both files and database
10619  curl -H "Authorization: Bearer <TOKEN>" \
10620    -H "Content-Type: application/json" \
10621    -X POST "https://orthodoxmetrics.com/api/backup/run" \
10622    -d '{"kind":"both","filterIds":[1,2]}'
10623  # With SSE streaming
10624  curl -H "Authorization: Bearer <TOKEN>" \
10625    -H "Content-Type: application/json" \
10626    -H "Accept: text/event-stream" \
10627    -X POST "https://orthodoxmetrics.com/api/backup/run" \
10628    -d '{"kind":"both"}'
10629  ```
10630  #### `GET /api/backup/:jobId`
10631  Get job details with artifacts.
10632  ```bash
10633  curl -H "Authorization: Bearer <TOKEN>" \
10634    "https://orthodoxmetrics.com/api/backup/123"
10635  ```
10636  ### Manifests
10637  #### `GET /api/backup/:artifactId/manifest`
10638  Get artifact manifest as JSON.
10639  ```bash
10640  curl -H "Authorization: Bearer <TOKEN>" \
10641    "https://orthodoxmetrics.com/api/backup/456/manifest"
10642  ```
10643  #### `GET /api/backup/:artifactId/manifest-text`
10644  Get artifact manifest as text.
10645  ```bash
10646  curl -H "Authorization: Bearer <TOKEN>" \
10647    "https://orthodoxmetrics.com/api/backup/456/manifest-text"
10648  ```
10649  ### Diffs
10650  #### `GET /api/backup/tags?scope=files`
10651  List available tags for diffs.
10652  ```bash
10653  curl -H "Authorization: Bearer <TOKEN>" \
10654    "https://orthodoxmetrics.com/api/backup/tags?scope=files"
10655  ```
10656  #### `GET /api/backup/diff`
10657  Generate diff between backup tags.
10658  ```bash
10659  curl -H "Authorization: Bearer <TOKEN>" \
10660    "https://orthodoxmetrics.com/api/backup/diff?fromTag=files-20251005-140000&toTag=files-20251005-153000&scope=files"
10661  ```
10662  ### Restoration
10663  #### `POST /api/backup/restore`
10664  Restore from backup.
10665  ```bash
10666  # Safe mode (default) - restore to separate location
10667  curl -H "Authorization: Bearer <TOKEN>" \
10668    -H "Content-Type: application/json" \
10669    -X POST "https://orthodoxmetrics.com/api/backup/restore" \
10670    -d '{"artifactId":123,"mode":"files"}'
10671  # Dangerous mode - restore in place (requires confirmation)
10672  curl -H "Authorization: Bearer <TOKEN>" \
10673    -H "Content-Type: application/json" \
10674    -X POST "https://orthodoxmetrics.com/api/backup/restore" \
10675    -d '{
10676      "artifactId":123,
10677      "mode":"files",
10678      "confirm":true,
10679      "overwriteTarget":true,
10680      "confirmationPhrase":"I UNDERSTAND"
10681    }'
10682  ```
10683  ### Filters
10684  #### `GET /api/backup/filters?scope=files&activeOnly=true`
10685  Get backup filters.
10686  ```bash
10687  curl -H "Authorization: Bearer <TOKEN>" \
10688    "https://orthodoxmetrics.com/api/backup/filters?scope=files"
10689  ```
10690  #### `POST /api/backup/filters`
10691  Create backup filter.
10692  ```bash
10693  curl -H "Authorization: Bearer <TOKEN>" \
10694    -H "Content-Type: application/json" \
10695    -X POST "https://orthodoxmetrics.com/api/backup/filters" \
10696    -d '{
10697      "scope":"files",
10698      "label":"Exclude Node Modules",
10699      "exclude_regex":"node_modules/",
10700      "is_active":true
10701    }'
10702  ```
10703  #### `PUT /api/backup/filters/:id`
10704  Update backup filter.
10705  ```bash
10706  curl -H "Authorization: Bearer <TOKEN>" \
10707    -H "Content-Type: application/json" \
10708    -X PUT "https://orthodoxmetrics.com/api/backup/filters/1" \
10709    -d '{"is_active":false}'
10710  ```
10711  #### `DELETE /api/backup/filters/:id`
10712  Delete backup filter.
10713  ```bash
10714  curl -H "Authorization: Bearer <TOKEN>" \
10715    -X DELETE "https://orthodoxmetrics.com/api/backup/filters/1"
10716  ```
10717  ## File Structure
10718  ```
10719  /var/backups/orthodoxmetrics/
10720  ├── prod/                           # Backup artifacts
10721  │   ├── 20251005-140000-file-backup.tgz
10722  │   ├── 20251005-140000-file-manifest.json
10723  │   ├── 20251005-140000-file-manifest.txt
10724  │   ├── 20251005-140000-orthodoxmetrics_db-backup.sql.gz
10725  │   ├── 20251005-140000-db-manifest.json
10726  │   └── 20251005-140000-db-manifest.txt
10727  └── .index.git/                     # Git index for manifests
10728      └── manifests/
10729          ├── 20251005-140000-files/
10730          │   ├── manifest.json
10731          │   └── manifest.txt
10732          └── 20251005-140000-db/
10733              ├── manifest.json
10734              └── manifest.txt
10735  ```
10736  ## Database Schema
10737  The system uses these tables:
10738  - `backup_jobs`: Job records with status and metadata
10739  - `backup_artifacts`: File artifacts linked to jobs
10740  - `backup_filters`: Regex filters for file inclusion/exclusion
10741  ## Configuration
10742  Edit `server/config/backup.ts`:
10743  ```typescript
10744  export const backupConfig = {
10745    basePathFiles: "/var/www/orthodoxmetrics/prod",
10746    backupOutDir: "/var/backups/orthodoxmetrics/prod", 
10747    gitIndexDir: "/var/backups/orthodoxmetrics/.index.git",
10748    mysqldumpBin: "/usr/bin/mysqldump",
10749    gzipLevel: 9,
10750    diff: {
10751      enableTableCountsQuickMode: true
10752    }
10753  };
10754  ```
10755  ## Security
10756  - All endpoints require `super_admin` role
10757  - Regex patterns are validated and catastrophic patterns rejected
10758  - Symlinks outside base path are ignored
10759  - Restoration requires explicit confirmation for dangerous operations
10760  - Confirmation phrase: `"I UNDERSTAND"`
10761  ## Cleanup
10762  Run cleanup to remove legacy backup code:
10763  ```bash
10764  # Dry run
10765  node server/src/modules/backup/cleanup.js dry-run
10766  # Apply changes
10767  node server/src/modules/backup/cleanup.js apply
10768  ```
10769  ## Troubleshooting
10770  ### MySQL Connection Issues
10771  Ensure the database user has sufficient privileges:
10772  ```sql
10773  GRANT SELECT, LOCK TABLES, SHOW VIEW, EVENT, TRIGGER ON *.* TO 'orthodoxapps'@'%';
10774  ```
10775  ### Permission Issues
10776  Ensure backup directories are writable:
10777  ```bash
10778  sudo mkdir -p /var/backups/orthodoxmetrics/prod
10779  sudo chown -R orthodoxapps:orthodoxapps /var/backups/orthodoxmetrics
10780  ```
10781  ### Git Issues
10782  Initialize the git repository manually if needed:
10783  ```bash
10784  cd /var/backups/orthodoxmetrics/.index.git
10785  git init
10786  git config user.name "OrthodoxMetrics Backup System"
10787  git config user.email "backup@orthodoxmetrics.com"
10788  ```
10789  ## Development
10790  ### Running Tests
10791  ```bash
10792  cd server
10793  npm test -- src/modules/backup/
10794  ```
10795  ### Type Checking
10796  ```bash
10797  cd server
10798  npx tsc --noEmit
10799  ```

10802  import React, { useState, useEffect } from 'react';

10836    PlayArrow as RunIcon,
10837    Refresh as RefreshIcon,
10838    Download as DownloadIcon,
10839    Restore as RestoreIcon,
10840    FilterList as FilterIcon,
10841    Compare as CompareIcon,
10842    Info as InfoIcon,
10843    Delete as DeleteIcon,
10844    Add as AddIcon
10845  } from '@mui/icons-material';
10846  import { DataGrid, GridColDef } from '@mui/x-data-grid';
10847  interface BackupJob {
10848    id: string;
10849    kind: 'files' | 'db' | 'both';
10850    status: 'queued' | 'running' | 'success' | 'failed';
10851    requested_by: number;
10852    started_at?: string;
10853    finished_at?: string;
10854    duration_ms?: number;
10855    error?: string;
10856    created_at: string;
10857  }
10858  interface BackupArtifact {
10859    id: string;
10860    job_id: string;
10861    artifact_type: 'files' | 'db';
10862    path: string;
10863    size_bytes?: number;
10864    manifest_path?: string;
10865    sha256?: string;
10866    created_at: string;
10867  }
10868  interface BackupFilter {
10869    id: string;
10870    scope: 'files' | 'db';
10871    label: string;
10872    include_regex?: string;
10873    exclude_regex?: string;
10874    is_active: boolean;
10875    created_at: string;
10876    updated_at: string;
10877  }
10878  const BackupDashboard: React.FC = () => {
10879    const [activeTab, setActiveTab] = useState(0);
10880    const [jobs, setJobs] = useState<BackupJob[]>([]);
10881    const [artifacts, setArtifacts] = useState<BackupArtifact[]>([]);
10882    const [filters, setFilters] = useState<BackupFilter[]>([]);
10883    const [loading, setLoading] = useState(false);
10884    const [error, setError] = useState<string | null>(null);
10885    const [success, setSuccess] = useState<string | null>(null);
10886    // Run backup form
10887    const [backupKind, setBackupKind] = useState<'files' | 'db' | 'both'>('both');
10888    const [selectedFilters, setSelectedFilters] = useState<string[]>([]);
10889    const [isRunning, setIsRunning] = useState(false);
10890    const [progress, setProgress] = useState(0);
10891    const [progressMessage, setProgressMessage] = useState('');
10892    // Filter dialog
10893    const [filterDialog, setFilterDialog] = useState(false);
10894    const [editingFilter, setEditingFilter] = useState<BackupFilter | null>(null);
10895    const [newFilter, setNewFilter] = useState({
10896      scope: 'files' as 'files' | 'db',
10897      label: '',
10898      include_regex: '',
10899      exclude_regex: '',
10900      is_active: true
10901    });
10902    // Diff dialog
10903    const [diffDialog, setDiffDialog] = useState(false);
10904    const [tags, setTags] = useState<string[]>([]);
10905    const [diffFrom, setDiffFrom] = useState('');
10906    const [diffTo, setDiffTo] = useState('');
10907    const [diffScope, setDiffScope] = useState<'files' | 'db'>('files');
10908    const [diffResult, setDiffResult] = useState<any>(null);
10909    useEffect(() => {
10910      loadData();
10911    }, []);
10912    const loadData = async () => {
10913      setLoading(true);
10914      try {
10915        const [jobsRes, filtersRes] = await Promise.all([
10916          fetch('/api/backup/recent'),
10917          fetch('/api/backup/filters')
10918        ]);
10919        if (jobsRes.ok) {
10920          const jobsData = await jobsRes.json();
10921          setJobs(jobsData.data.jobs || []);
10922          setArtifacts(jobsData.data.artifacts || []);
10923        }
10924        if (filtersRes.ok) {
10925          const filtersData = await filtersRes.json();
10926          setFilters(filtersData.data || []);
10927        }
10928      } catch (err) {
10929        setError('Failed to load backup data');
10930      } finally {
10931        setLoading(false);
10932      }
10933    };
10934    const runBackup = async () => {
10935      setIsRunning(true);
10936      setProgress(0);
10937      setProgressMessage('Starting backup...');
10938      setError(null);
10939      try {
10940        const response = await fetch('/api/backup/run', {
10941          method: 'POST',
10942          headers: {
10943            'Content-Type': 'application/json',
10944            'Accept': 'text/event-stream'
10945          },
10946          body: JSON.stringify({
10947            kind: backupKind,
10948            filterIds: selectedFilters.map(id => parseInt(id))
10949          })
10950        });
10951        if (!response.ok) {
10952          throw new Error('Failed to start backup');
10953        }
10954        // Handle SSE stream
10955        const reader = response.body?.getReader();
10956        if (reader) {
10957          while (true) {
10958            const { done, value } = await reader.read();
10959            if (done) break;
10960            const text = new TextDecoder().decode(value);
10961            const lines = text.split('\n');
10962            for (const line of lines) {
10963              if (line.startsWith('data: ')) {
10964                try {
10965                  const data = JSON.parse(line.slice(6));
10966                  if (data.final) {
10967                    setSuccess('Backup completed successfully!');
10968                    setProgress(100);
10969                    setProgressMessage('Completed');
10970                    loadData();
10971                    break;
10972                  } else if (data.error) {
10973                    throw new Error(data.message);
10974                  } else {
10975                    setProgress(data.pct || 0);
10976                    setProgressMessage(data.message || '');
10977                  }
10978                } catch (e) {
10979                  // Ignore JSON parse errors for incomplete data
10980                }
10981              }
10982            }
10983          }
10984        }
10985      } catch (err) {
10986        setError(err instanceof Error ? err.message : 'Backup failed');
10987      } finally {
10988        setIsRunning(false);
10989      }
10990    };
10991    const createFilter = async () => {
10992      try {
10993        const response = await fetch('/api/backup/filters', {
10994          method: 'POST',
10995          headers: { 'Content-Type': 'application/json' },
10996          body: JSON.stringify(newFilter)
10997        });
10998        if (!response.ok) {
10999          throw new Error('Failed to create filter');
11000        }
11001        setSuccess('Filter created successfully');
11002        setFilterDialog(false);
11003        setNewFilter({
11004          scope: 'files',
11005          label: '',
11006          include_regex: '',
11007          exclude_regex: '',
11008          is_active: true
11009        });
11010        loadData();
11011      } catch (err) {
11012        setError(err instanceof Error ? err.message : 'Failed to create filter');
11013      }
11014    };
11015    const generateDiff = async () => {
11016      try {
11017        const response = await fetch(
11018          `/api/backup/diff?fromTag=${diffFrom}&toTag=${diffTo}&scope=${diffScope}`
11019        );
11020        if (!response.ok) {
11021          throw new Error('Failed to generate diff');
11022        }
11023        const data = await response.json();
11024        setDiffResult(data.data);
11025      } catch (err) {
11026        setError(err instanceof Error ? err.message : 'Failed to generate diff');
11027      }
11028    };
11029    const loadTags = async () => {
11030      try {
11031        const response = await fetch(`/api/backup/tags?scope=${diffScope}`);
11032        if (response.ok) {
11033          const data = await response.json();
11034          setTags(data.data || []);
11035        }
11036      } catch (err) {
11037        console.error('Failed to load tags:', err);
11038      }
11039    };
11040    const jobColumns: GridColDef[] = [
11041      { field: 'id', headerName: 'ID', width: 80 },
11042      { 
11043        field: 'kind', 
11044        headerName: 'Type', 
11045        width: 100,
11046        renderCell: (params) => (
11047          <Chip 
11048            label={params.value} 
11049            size="small"
11050            color={params.value === 'both' ? 'primary' : 'default'}
11051          />
11052        )
11053      },
11054      { 
11055        field: 'status', 
11056        headerName: 'Status', 
11057        width: 120,
11058        renderCell: (params) => (
11059          <Chip 
11060            label={params.value} 
11061            size="small"
11062            color={
11063              params.value === 'success' ? 'success' :
11064              params.value === 'failed' ? 'error' :
11065              params.value === 'running' ? 'warning' : 'default'
11066            }
11067          />
11068        )
11069      },

11516  const BackupDetails: React.FC = () => {
11517    const { jobId } = useParams<{ jobId: string }>();

11519

11521    const [artifacts, setArtifacts] = useState<BackupArtifact[]>([]);
11522    const [loading, setLoading] = useState(true);
11523    const [error, setError] = useState<string | null>(null);
11524    const [success, setSuccess] = useState<string | null>(null);
11525    // Manifest dialog
11526    const [manifestDialog, setManifestDialog] = useState(false);
11527    const [manifestContent, setManifestContent] = useState<any>(null);
11528    const [manifestType, setManifestType] = useState<'json' | 'text'>('json');
11529    // Restore dialog
11530    const [restoreDialog, setRestoreDialog] = useState(false);
11531    const [selectedArtifact, setSelectedArtifact] = useState<BackupArtifact | null>(null);
11532    const [restoreMode, setRestoreMode] = useState<'files' | 'db'>('files');
11533    const [overwriteTarget, setOverwriteTarget] = useState(false);
11534    const [confirmRestore, setConfirmRestore] = useState(false);
11535    const [confirmationPhrase, setConfirmationPhrase] = useState('');
11536    useEffect(() => {
11537      if (jobId) {
11538        loadJobDetails();
11539      }
11540    }, [jobId]);
11541    const loadJobDetails = async () => {
11542      setLoading(true);
11543      try {
11544        const response = await fetch(`/api/backup/${jobId}`);
11545        
11546        if (!response.ok) {
11547          throw new Error('Failed to load job details');
11548        }
11549        const data = await response.json();
11550        setJob(data.data.job);
11551        setArtifacts(data.data.artifacts || []);
11552      } catch (err) {
11553        setError(err instanceof Error ? err.message : 'Failed to load job details');
11554      } finally {
11555        setLoading(false);
11556      }
11557    };
11558    const viewManifest = async (artifact: BackupArtifact, type: 'json' | 'text') => {
11559      try {
11560        const endpoint = type === 'json' ? 'manifest' : 'manifest-text';
11561        const response = await fetch(`/api/backup/${artifact.id}/${endpoint}`);
11562        
11563        if (!response.ok) {
11564          throw new Error('Failed to load manifest');
11565        }
11566        if (type === 'json') {
11567          const data = await response.json();
11568          setManifestContent(data.data);
11569        } else {
11570          const text = await response.text();
11571          setManifestContent(text);
11572        }
11573        
11574        setManifestType(type);
11575        setManifestDialog(true);
11576      } catch (err) {
11577        setError(err instanceof Error ? err.message : 'Failed to load manifest');
11578      }
11579    };
11580    const copyToClipboard = async (text: string) => {
11581      try {
11582        await navigator.clipboard.writeText(text);
11583        setSuccess('Copied to clipboard');
11584      } catch (err) {
11585        setError('Failed to copy to clipboard');
11586      }
11587    };
11588    const openRestoreDialog = (artifact: BackupArtifact) => {
11589      setSelectedArtifact(artifact);
11590      setRestoreMode(artifact.artifact_type);
11591      setOverwriteTarget(false);
11592      setConfirmRestore(false);
11593      setConfirmationPhrase('');
11594      setRestoreDialog(true);
11595    };
11596    const executeRestore = async () => {
11597      if (!selectedArtifact) return;
11598      try {
11599        const response = await fetch('/api/backup/restore', {
11600          method: 'POST',
11601          headers: { 'Content-Type': 'application/json' },
11602          body: JSON.stringify({
11603            artifactId: parseInt(selectedArtifact.id),
11604            mode: restoreMode,
11605            confirm: confirmRestore,
11606            overwriteTarget,
11607            confirmationPhrase: overwriteTarget ? confirmationPhrase : undefined
11608          })
11609        });
11610        if (!response.ok) {
11611          const errorData = await response.json();
11612          throw new Error(errorData.details || 'Restore failed');
11613        }
11614        const data = await response.json();
11615        setSuccess(data.data.message);
11616        setRestoreDialog(false);
11617      } catch (err) {
11618        setError(err instanceof Error ? err.message : 'Restore failed');
11619      }
11620    };
11621    const formatBytes = (bytes?: number) => {
11622      if (!bytes) return 'Unknown';
11623      const mb = bytes / (1024 * 1024);
11624      if (mb < 1024) {
11625        return `${mb.toFixed(1)} MB`;
11626      }
11627      return `${(mb / 1024).toFixed(1)} GB`;
11628    };
11629    const formatDuration = (ms?: number) => {
11630      if (!ms) return 'Unknown';
11631      const seconds = Math.floor(ms / 1000);
11632      const minutes = Math.floor(seconds / 60);
11633      if (minutes > 0) {
11634        return `${minutes}m ${seconds % 60}s`;
11635      }
11636      return `${seconds}s`;
11637    };
11638    const getStatusColor = (status: string) => {

11640        case 'success': return 'success';
11641        case 'failed': return 'error';
11642        case 'running': return 'warning';
11643        default: return 'default';
11644      }
11645    };
11646    if (loading) {
11647      return (
11648        <Box sx={{ p: 3 }}>
11649          <Typography>Loading job details...</Typography>
11650        </Box>
11651      );
11652    }
11653    if (!job) {
11654      return (
11655        <Box sx={{ p: 3 }}>
11656          <Typography color="error">Job not found</Typography>
11657          <Button startIcon={<BackIcon />} onClick={() => navigate(-1)} sx={{ mt: 2 }}>

11667            <BackIcon />
11668          </IconButton>
11669          <Typography variant="h4">
11670            Backup Job #{job.id}
11671          </Typography>
11672        </Box>
11673        {error && (
11674          <Alert severity="error" sx={{ mb: 2 }} onClose={() => setError(null)}>
11675            {error}
11676          </Alert>
11677        )}
11678        {success && (
11679          <Alert severity="success" sx={{ mb: 2 }} onClose={() => setSuccess(null)}>
11680            {success}
11681          </Alert>
11682        )}
11683        <Grid container spacing={3}>
11684          {/* Job Details */}
11685          <Grid item xs={12} md={6}>
11686            <Card>
11687              <CardContent>
11688                <Typography variant="h6" gutterBottom>
11689                  Job Details
11690                </Typography>
11691

11776                    </>
11777                  )}
11778                  {job.error && (
11779                    <>
11780                      <Divider />
11781                      <ListItem>
11782                        <ListItemText
11783                          primary="Error"
11784                          secondary={
11785                            <Typography color="error" variant="body2">
11786                              {job.error}
11787                            </Typography>
11788                          }
11789                        />
11790                      </ListItem>
11791                    </>
11792                  )}
11793                </List>
11794              </CardContent>
11795            </Card>
11796          </Grid>
11797          {/* Artifacts */}
11798          <Grid item xs={12} md={6}>
11799            <Card>
11800              <CardContent>
11801                <Typography variant="h6" gutterBottom>
11802                  Backup Artifacts ({artifacts.length})
11803                </Typography>
11804                {artifacts.length === 0 ? (
11805                  <Typography color="textSecondary">
11806                    No artifacts found for this job.
11807                  </Typography>
11808                ) : (
11809                  artifacts.map((artifact) => (
11810                    <Paper key={artifact.id} sx={{ p: 2, mb: 2 }}>
11811                      <Box sx={{ display: 'flex', justifyContent: 'space-between', alignItems: 'flex-start', mb: 1 }}>
11812                        <Typography variant="subtitle1">
11813                          {artifact.artifact_type.toUpperCase()} Backup
11814                        </Typography>
11815                        <Chip 
11816                          label={artifact.artifact_type} 
11817                          size="small"
11818                          color={artifact.artifact_type === 'files' ? 'primary' : 'secondary'}
11819                        />
11820                      </Box>
11821                      <Typography variant="body2" color="textSecondary" sx={{ mb: 1 }}>
11822                        Path: {artifact.path}
11823                      </Typography>
11824                      <Typography variant="body2" color="textSecondary" sx={{ mb: 1 }}>
11825                        Size: {formatBytes(artifact.size_bytes)}
11826                      </Typography>
11827                      <Typography variant="body2" color="textSecondary" sx={{ mb: 1 }}>
11828                        Created: {new Date(artifact.created_at).toLocaleString()}
11829                      </Typography>
11830                      {artifact.sha256 && (
11831                        <Box sx={{ display: 'flex', alignItems: 'center', mb: 2 }}>
11832                          <Typography variant="body2" color="textSecondary" sx={{ mr: 1 }}>
11833                            SHA256: {artifact.sha256.substring(0, 16)}...
11834                          </Typography>
11835                          <IconButton 
11836                            size="small" 
11837                            onClick={() => copyToClipboard(artifact.sha256!)}
11838                          >
11839                            <CopyIcon fontSize="small" />
11840                          </IconButton>
11841                        </Box>
11842                      )}
11843                      <Box sx={{ display: 'flex', gap: 1, flexWrap: 'wrap' }}>
11844                        <Button
11845                          size="small"
11846                          startIcon={<ViewIcon />}
11847                          onClick={() => viewManifest(artifact, 'json')}
11848                        >
11849                          JSON Manifest
11850                        </Button>
11851                        
11852                        <Button
11853                          size="small"
11854                          startIcon={<ViewIcon />}
11855                          onClick={() => viewManifest(artifact, 'text')}
11856                        >
11857                          Text Manifest
11858                        </Button>
11859                        <Button
11860                          size="small"
11861                          startIcon={<RestoreIcon />}
11862                          onClick={() => openRestoreDialog(artifact)}
11863                          color="warning"
11864                        >
11865                          Restore
11866                        </Button>
11867                      </Box>
11868                    </Paper>
11869                  ))
11870                )}
11871              </CardContent>
11872            </Card>
11873          </Grid>
11874        </Grid>
11875        {/* Manifest Dialog */}
11876        <Dialog 
11877          open={manifestDialog} 
11878          onClose={() => setManifestDialog(false)} 
11879          maxWidth="md" 
11880          fullWidth
11881        >
11882          <DialogTitle>
11883            {manifestType === 'json' ? 'JSON Manifest' : 'Text Manifest'}
11884          </DialogTitle>
11885          <DialogContent>
11886            <pre style={{ 
11887              background: '#f5f5f5', 
11888              padding: '1rem', 
11889              overflow: 'auto',
11890              maxHeight: '400px',
11891              fontSize: '12px'
11892            }}>
11893              {manifestType === 'json' 
11894                ? JSON.stringify(manifestContent, null, 2)
11895                : manifestContent
11896              }
11897            </pre>
11898          </DialogContent>
11899          <DialogActions>
11900            <Button 
11901              onClick={() => copyToClipboard(
11902                manifestType === 'json' 
11903                  ? JSON.stringify(manifestContent, null, 2)
11904                  : manifestContent
11905              )}
11906            >
11907              Copy
11908            </Button>
11909            <Button onClick={() => setManifestDialog(false)}>Close</Button>
11910          </DialogActions>
11911        </Dialog>
11912        {/* Restore Dialog */}
11913        <Dialog 
11914          open={restoreDialog} 
11915          onClose={() => setRestoreDialog(false)} 
11916          maxWidth="sm" 
11917          fullWidth
11918        >
11919          <DialogTitle>
11920            Restore {selectedArtifact?.artifact_type.toUpperCase()} Backup
11921          </DialogTitle>
11922          <DialogContent>
11923            <Typography variant="body2" color="textSecondary" sx={{ mb: 2 }}>
11924              Artifact: {selectedArtifact?.path}
11925            </Typography>
11926            <FormControlLabel
11927              control={
11928                <Checkbox
11929                  checked={overwriteTarget}
11930                  onChange={(e) => setOverwriteTarget(e.target.checked)}
11931                />
11932              }
11933              label="Overwrite target (DANGEROUS)"
11934              sx={{ mb: 2 }}
11935            />
11936            {overwriteTarget && (
11937              <>
11938                <Alert severity="warning" sx={{ mb: 2 }}>
11939                  You are about to restore directly to the original location. 
11940                  This will overwrite existing data!
11941                </Alert>
11942                <FormControlLabel
11943                  control={
11944                    <Checkbox
11945                      checked={confirmRestore}
11946                      onChange={(e) => setConfirmRestore(e.target.checked)}
11947                    />
11948                  }
11949                  label="I understand the risks"
11950                  sx={{ mb: 2 }}
11951                />
11952                {confirmRestore && (
11953                  <TextField
11954                    fullWidth
11955                    label="Type 'I UNDERSTAND' to confirm"
11956                    value={confirmationPhrase}
11957                    onChange={(e) => setConfirmationPhrase(e.target.value)}
11958                    sx={{ mb: 2 }}
11959                  />
11960                )}
11961              </>
11962            )}
11963            {!overwriteTarget && (
11964              <Alert severity="info" sx={{ mb: 2 }}>
11965                Safe mode: Will restore to a separate location without overwriting existing data.
11966              </Alert>
11967            )}
11968          </DialogContent>
11969          <DialogActions>
11970            <Button onClick={() => setRestoreDialog(false)}>Cancel</Button>
11971            <Button 
11972              onClick={executeRestore}
11973              variant="contained"
11974              color={overwriteTarget ? "error" : "primary"}
11975              disabled={
11976                overwriteTarget && 
11977                (!confirmRestore || confirmationPhrase !== 'I UNDERSTAND')
11978              }
11979            >
11980              {overwriteTarget ? 'Restore (OVERWRITE)' : 'Restore (SAFE)'}
11981            </Button>
11982          </DialogActions>
11983        </Dialog>
11984      </Box>
11985    );
11986  };
11987  export default BackupDetails;
11988  EOF
