12066  const express = require('express');
12067  const router = express.Router();
12068  // Middleware to ensure super_admin role
12069  const requireSuperAdmin = (req, res, next) => {
12070    if (!req.session?.user) {
12071      return res.status(401).json({ error: 'Authentication required' });
12072    }
12073    
12074    if (req.session.user.role !== 'super_admin') {
12075      return res.status(403).json({ error: 'Super admin access required' });
12076    }
12077    
12078    next();
12079  };
12080  // Apply super admin middleware to all routes
12081  router.use(requireSuperAdmin);
12082  // GET /api/backup/status - Get system status
12083  router.get('/status', async (req, res) => {
12084    try {
12085      res.json({
12086        status: 'active',
12087        version: '1.0.0',
12088        timestamp: new Date().toISOString(),
12089        message: 'Backup system operational'
12090      });
12091    } catch (error) {
12092      console.error('Status check failed:', error);
12093      res.status(500).json({ error: 'Failed to get system status' });
12094    }
12095  });
12096  // GET /api/backup/jobs - List backup jobs
12097  router.get('/jobs', async (req, res) => {
12098    try {
12099      res.json([]);
12100    } catch (error) {
12101      console.error('Failed to list backup jobs:', error);
12102      res.status(500).json({ error: 'Failed to list backup jobs' });
12103    }
12104  });
12105  module.exports = router;
12106  EOF

12281  cat > /var/www/orthodoxmetrics/prod/server/src/modules/backup/backup.routes.js << 'EOF'
12282  const express = require('express');
12283  const router = express.Router();
12284  const BackupEngine = require('./BackupEngine');
12285  const fs = require('fs').promises;
12286  const path = require('path');
12287  // Initialize backup engine (will be done in main app)
12288  let backupEngine = null;
12289  const initializeBackupEngine = (db) => {
12290    if (!backupEngine) {
12291      backupEngine = new BackupEngine(db, {
12292        backupRoot: '/var/backups/orthodoxmetrics',
12293        prodRoot: '/var/www/orthodoxmetrics/prod',
12294        database: {
12295          host: process.env.DB_HOST || 'localhost',
12296          user: process.env.DB_USER || 'orthodoxmetrics_user',
12297          password: process.env.DB_PASSWORD,
12298          database: process.env.DB_NAME || 'orthodoxmetrics_db'
12299        }
12300      });
12301      backupEngine.initialize().catch(console.error);
12302    }
12303    return backupEngine;
12304  };
12305  // Middleware to ensure super_admin role
12306  const requireSuperAdmin = (req, res, next) => {
12307    if (!req.session?.user) {
12308      return res.status(401).json({ error: 'Authentication required' });
12309    }
12310    if (req.session.user.role !== 'super_admin') {
12311      return res.status(403).json({ error: 'Super admin access required' });
12312    }
12313    next();
12314  };
12315  // Middleware to initialize backup engine
12316  const ensureBackupEngine = (req, res, next) => {
12317    if (!backupEngine) {
12318      // Get database connection from app context
12319      const db = req.app.get('db');
12320      if (!db) {
12321        return res.status(500).json({ error: 'Database connection not available' });
12322      }
12323      initializeBackupEngine(db);
12324    }
12325    next();
12326  };
12327  // Apply middleware to all routes
12328  router.use(requireSuperAdmin);
12329  router.use(ensureBackupEngine);
12330  // GET /api/backup/status - Get system status
12331  router.get('/status', async (req, res) => {
12332    try {
12333      const diskUsage = await getDiskUsage();
12334      res.json({
12335        status: 'active',
12336        version: '1.0.0',
12337        timestamp: new Date().toISOString(),
12338        message: 'Backup system operational',
12339        diskUsage: diskUsage
12340      });
12341    } catch (error) {
12342      console.error('Status check failed:', error);
12343      res.status(500).json({ error: 'Failed to get system status' });
12344    }
12345  });
12346  // GET /api/backup/jobs - List backup jobs
12347  router.get('/jobs', async (req, res) => {
12348    try {
12349      const page = parseInt(req.query.page) || 1;
12350      const limit = parseInt(req.query.limit) || 20;
12351      
12352      const jobs = await backupEngine.getJobs(page, limit);
12353      res.json({ jobs, page, limit });
12354    } catch (error) {
12355      console.error('Failed to list backup jobs:', error);
12356      res.status(500).json({ error: 'Failed to list backup jobs' });
12357    }
12358  });
12359  // POST /api/backup/create - Create new backup job
12360  router.post('/create', async (req, res) => {
12361    try {
12362      const { kind, filters } = req.body;
12363      
12364      // Validate input
12365      if (!kind || !['files', 'db', 'both'].includes(kind)) {
12366        return res.status(400).json({ error: 'Invalid backup kind. Must be: files, db, or both' });
12367      }
12368      const requestedBy = req.session.user.username || req.session.user.email;
12369      const result = await backupEngine.createBackupJob(kind, requestedBy, filters || {});
12370      
12371      res.json(result);
12372    } catch (error) {
12373      console.error('Failed to create backup job:', error);
12374      res.status(500).json({ error: 'Failed to create backup job' });
12375    }
12376  });
12377  module.exports = router;
12378  EOF

AND church_id = ? AND table_name = ? ORDER BY updated_at DESC LIMIT 1\",\n      [userId, churchId, table]\n    );\n\n    if (rows.length === 0) {\n      return res.json({\n        success: true,\n        data: {\n          columns: { visible: [], order: [] },\n          autoHideEmpty: false,\n          defaultSort: { field: \"\", order: \"desc\" }\n        }\n      });\n    }\n\n    const settings = JSON.parse(rows[0].settings_json);\n    res.json({ success: true, data: settings });\n\n  } catch (error) {\n    console.error(\"Error fetching table settings:\", error);\n    res.status(500).json({ success: false, error: \"Failed to fetch table settings\" });\n  }\n});\n\n// POST /api/settings/table-view - Save user table view settings\nrouter.post(\"/table-view\", async (req, res) => {\n  try {\n    const { churchId, table, settings } = req.body;\n    const userId = req.session?.user?.id;\n\n    if (!userId) {\n      return res.status(401).json({ success: false, error: \"Authentication required\" });\n    }\n\n    if (!churchId || !table || !settings) {\n      return res.status(400).json({ success: false, error: \"churchId, table, and settings are required\" });\n    }\n\n    // Validate settings structure\n    if (!settings.columns || !settings.defaultSort) {\n      return res.status(400).json({ success: false, error: \"Invalid settings structure\" });\n    }\n\n    const settingsJson = JSON.stringify(settings);\n\n    // Check if settings already exist\n    const [existingRows] = await getAppPool().query(\n      \"SELECT id FROM user_table_settings WHERE user_id = ? AND church_id = ? AND table_name = ?\",\n      [userId, churchId, table]\n    );\n\n    if (existingRows.length > 0) {\n      // Update existing settings\n      await getAppPool().query(\n        \"UPDATE user_table_settings SET settings_json = ?, updated_at = NOW() WHERE user_id = ? AND church_id = ? AND table_name = ?\",\n        [settingsJson, userId, churchId, table]\n      );\n    } else {\n      // Insert new settings\n      await getAppPool().query(\n        \"INSERT INTO user_table_settings (user_id, church_id, table_name, settings_json, created_at, updated_at) VALUES (?, ?, ?, ?, NOW(), NOW())\",\n        [userId, churchId, table, settingsJson]\n      );\n    }\n\n    console.log(`✅ Table settings saved for user ${userId}, church ${churchId}, table ${table}`);\n\n    res.json({\n      success: true,\n      message: \"Table settings saved successfully\",\n      data: settings\n    });\n\n  } catch (error) {\n    console.error(\"Error saving table settings:\", error);\n    res.status(500).json({ success: false, error: \"Failed to save table settings\" });\n  }\n});\n' api/settings.js

12654  const fs = require('fs');
12655  // Read the file
12656  let content = fs.readFileSync('BaptismRecordsPage.tsx', 'utf8');
12657  // Find the line with getColumnDefinitions and add the functions after it
12658  const functionsToAdd = `
12659  const getColumnDefinitions = (recordType: string) => {
12660    return safeColumnsFor(recordType);
12661  };
12662  // Function to check if a column has any non-empty data
12663  const hasColumnData = (records: any[], field: string) => {
12664    return records.some(record => {
12665      const value = record[field];
12666      return value && value.toString().trim() !== "" && value !== "N/A" && value !== null && value !== undefined;
12667    });
12668  };
12669  // Function to get hidden fields based on empty data
12670  const getHiddenFields = (records: any[], autoHide: boolean) => {
12671    if (!autoHide) return [];
12672    
12673    const hiddenFields = [];
12674    const allFields = getColumnDefinitions(selectedRecordType).map(col => col.field);
12675    
12676    for (const field of allFields) {
12677      if (!hasColumnData(records, field)) {
12678        hiddenFields.push(field);
12679      }
12680    }
12681    
12682    return hiddenFields;
12683  };
12684  `;
12685  // Find where to insert (after the last import or before the component)
12686  const insertPoint = content.indexOf('const BaptismRecordsPage: React.FC = () => {');
12687  if (insertPoint !== -1) {
12688    content = content.slice(0, insertPoint) + functionsToAdd + '\n' + content.slice(insertPoint);
12689    fs.writeFileSync('BaptismRecordsPage.tsx', content);
12690    console.log('Functions added successfully');
12691  } else {
12692    console.log('Could not find insert point');
12693  }

12713  import React, { useState, useEffect } from 'react';
12714  import {
12715    Dialog, DialogTitle, DialogContent, DialogActions, Button, Box, Typography,
12716    FormControl, InputLabel, Select, MenuItem, FormControlLabel, Checkbox,
12717    RadioGroup, Radio, Divider, Stack, Chip, IconButton, Tooltip, Alert, CircularProgress,
12718    Switch, Grid
12719  } from '@mui/material';
12720  import { Close as CloseIcon, Visibility as VisibilityIcon, VisibilityOff as VisibilityOffIcon } from '@mui/icons-material';
12721  interface ColumnConfig {
12722    field: string;
12723    headerName: string;
12724    visible: boolean;
12725    order: number;
12726  }
12727  interface TableSettings {
12728    columns: {
12729      visible: string[];
12730      order: string[];
12731    };
12732    autoHideEmpty: boolean;
12733    defaultSort: {
12734      field: string;
12735      order: 'asc' | 'desc';
12736    };
12737  }
12738  interface CustomizeTableDialogProps {
12739    open: boolean;
12740    onClose: () => void;
12741    onSave: (settings: TableSettings) => void;
12742    columns: ColumnConfig[];
12743    currentSettings?: TableSettings;
12744    title?: string;
12745    churchId: number;
12746    tableName: string;
12747  }
12748  const CustomizeTableDialog: React.FC<CustomizeTableDialogProps> = ({
12749    open, onClose, onSave, columns, currentSettings, title = 'Customize Table', churchId, tableName
12750  }) => {
12751    const [localSettings, setLocalSettings] = useState<TableSettings>({
12752      columns: {
12753        visible: columns.map(col => col.field),
12754        order: columns.map(col => col.field)
12755      },
12756      autoHideEmpty: false,
12757      defaultSort: {
12758        field: columns[0]?.field || '',
12759        order: 'desc'
12760      }
12761    });
12762    const [loading, setLoading] = useState(false);
12763    const [saving, setSaving] = useState(false);
12764    const [error, setError] = useState<string | null>(null);
12765    useEffect(() => {
12766      if (open && churchId && tableName) {
12767        loadSettings();
12768      }
12769    }, [open, churchId, tableName]);
12770    const loadSettings = async () => {
12771      setLoading(true);
12772      setError(null);
12773      try {
12774        // For now, use default settings since we don't have the API yet
12775        const defaultSettings = {
12776          columns: {
12777            visible: columns.map(col => col.field),
12778            order: columns.map(col => col.field)
12779          },
12780          autoHideEmpty: false,
12781          defaultSort: {
12782            field: columns[0]?.field || '',
12783            order: 'desc' as 'asc' | 'desc'
12784          }
12785        };
12786        setLocalSettings(defaultSettings);
12787      } catch (err) {
12788        console.error('Error loading settings:', err);
12789        setError('Failed to load settings');
12790      } finally {
12791        setLoading(false);
12792      }
12793    };
12794    const handleColumnVisibilityChange = (field: string, visible: boolean) => {
12795      setLocalSettings(prev => ({
12796        ...prev,
12797        columns: {
12798          ...prev.columns,
12799          visible: visible
12800            ? [...prev.columns.visible, field]
12801            : prev.columns.visible.filter(f => f !== field)
12802        }
12803      }));
12804    };
12805    const handleAutoHideToggle = (event: React.ChangeEvent<HTMLInputElement>) => {
12806      setLocalSettings(prev => ({ ...prev, autoHideEmpty: event.target.checked }));
12807    };
12808    const handleDefaultSortFieldChange = (event: any) => {
12809      const field = event.target.value;
12810      setLocalSettings(prev => ({
12811        ...prev,
12812        defaultSort: { ...prev.defaultSort, field }
12813      }));
12814    };
12815    const handleDefaultSortOrderChange = (event: React.ChangeEvent<HTMLInputElement>) => {
12816      const order = event.target.value as 'asc' | 'desc';
12817      setLocalSettings(prev => ({
12818        ...prev,
12819        defaultSort: { ...prev.defaultSort, order }
12820      }));
12821    };
12822    const handleSave = async () => {
12823      setSaving(true);
12824      setError(null);
12825      try {
12826        // For now, just save locally
12827        console.log('Saving settings:', localSettings);
12828        onSave(localSettings);
12829        onClose();
12830      } catch (err) {
12831        console.error('Error saving settings:', err);
12832        setError('Failed to save settings');
12833      } finally {
12834        setSaving(false);
12835      }
12836    };
12837    const handleReset = () => {
12838      setLocalSettings({
12839        columns: {
12840          visible: columns.map(col => col.field),
12841          order: columns.map(col => col.field)
12842        },
12843        autoHideEmpty: false,
12844        defaultSort: {
12845          field: columns[0]?.field || '',
12846          order: 'desc'
12847        }
12848      });
12849    };
12850    return (
12851      <Dialog open={open} onClose={onClose} maxWidth="md" fullWidth>
12852        <DialogTitle>
12853          {title}
12854          <IconButton onClick={onClose} size="small" sx={{ position: 'absolute', right: 8, top: 8 }}>
12855            <CloseIcon />
12856          </IconButton>
12857        </DialogTitle>
12858        <DialogContent>
12859          {error && (
12860            <Alert severity="error" sx={{ mb: 2 }}>
12861              {error}
12862            </Alert>
12863          )}
12864          {loading ? (
12865            <Box sx={{ display: 'flex', justifyContent: 'center', p: 4 }}>
12866              <CircularProgress />
12867            </Box>
12868          ) : (
12869            <Stack spacing={3}>
12870              {/* Column Visibility Section */}
12871              <Box>
12872                <Typography variant="h6" gutterBottom>
12873                  Column Visibility
12874                  <Chip label="Persisted" size="small" color="primary" sx={{ ml: 1 }} />
12875                </Typography>
12876                <FormControlLabel
12877                  control={<Switch checked={localSettings.autoHideEmpty} onChange={handleAutoHideToggle} />}
12878                  label="Auto-hide empty fields"
12879                />
12880                <Divider sx={{ my: 2 }} />
12881                <Grid container spacing={1}>
12882                  {columns.map((col) => (
12883                    <Grid item xs={6} sm={4} md={3} key={col.field}>
12884                      <FormControlLabel
12885                        control={
12886                          <Checkbox
12887                            checked={localSettings.columns.visible.includes(col.field)}
12888                            onChange={(e) => handleColumnVisibilityChange(col.field, e.target.checked)}
12889                            icon={<VisibilityOffIcon fontSize="small" />}
12890                            checkedIcon={<VisibilityIcon fontSize="small" />}
12891                          />
12892                        }
12893                        label={
12894                          <Tooltip title={col.headerName}>
12895                            <Typography variant="body2" noWrap>{col.headerName}</Typography>
12896                          </Tooltip>
12897                        }
12898                      />
12899                    </Grid>
12900                  ))}
12901                </Grid>
12902              </Box>
12903              {/* Default Sort Section */}
12904              <Box>
12905                <Typography variant="h6" gutterBottom>
12906                  Default Sort
12907                  <Chip label="Persisted" size="small" color="primary" sx={{ ml: 1 }} />
12908                </Typography>
12909                <Stack direction="row" spacing={2} alignItems="center">
12910                  <FormControl sx={{ minWidth: 180 }}>
12911                    <InputLabel>Sort Field</InputLabel>
12912                    <Select
12913                      value={localSettings.defaultSort.field}
12914                      onChange={handleDefaultSortFieldChange}
12915                      label="Sort Field"
12916                    >
12917                      {columns.map(col => (
12918                        <MenuItem key={col.field} value={col.field}>{col.headerName}</MenuItem>
12919                      ))}
12920                    </Select>
12921                  </FormControl>
12922                  <FormControl>
12923                    <RadioGroup
12924                      row
12925                      name="default-sort-order"
12926                      value={localSettings.defaultSort.order}
12927                      onChange={handleDefaultSortOrderChange}
12928                    >
12929                      <FormControlLabel value="asc" control={<Radio />} label="Ascending" />
12930                      <FormControlLabel value="desc" control={<Radio />} label="Descending" />
12931                    </RadioGroup>
12932                  </FormControl>
12933                </Stack>
12934              </Box>
12935            </Stack>
12936          )}
12937        </DialogContent>
12938        <DialogActions sx={{ p: 2 }}>
12939          <Button onClick={handleReset} color="secondary">
12940            Reset to Defaults
12941          </Button>
12942          <Box sx={{ flex: 1 }} />
12943          <Button onClick={onClose} disabled={saving}>
12944            Cancel
12945          </Button>
12946          <Button onClick={handleSave} variant="contained" disabled={saving || loading}>
12947            {saving ? <CircularProgress size={20} /> : 'Save Settings'}
12948          </Button>
12949        </DialogActions>
12950      </Dialog>
12951    );
12952  };
12953  export default CustomizeTableDialog;
12954  EOF

12958  export interface TableSettings {
12959    columns: {
12960      visible: string[];
12961      order: string[];
12962    };
12963    autoHideEmpty: boolean;
12964    defaultSort: {
12965      field: string;
12966      order: 'asc' | 'desc';
12967    };
12968  }
12969  interface ApiResponse<T> {
12970    success: boolean;
12971    data?: T;
12972    error?: string;
12973    message?: string;
12974  }
12975  const BASE_URL = '/api/user-settings/table-view';
12976  export const userTableSettingsApi = {
12977    async getTableSettings(churchId: number, tableName: string): Promise<ApiResponse<TableSettings>> {
12978      try {
12979        const response = await fetch(`${BASE_URL}?churchId=${churchId}&tableName=${tableName}`);
12980        const data = await response.json();
12981        return data;
12982      } catch (error) {
12983        console.error('API Error fetching table settings:', error);
12984        return { success: false, error: 'Network error' };
12985      }
12986    },
12987    async saveTableSettings(churchId: number, tableName: string, settings: TableSettings): Promise<ApiResponse<null>> {
12988      try {
12989        const response = await fetch(BASE_URL, {
12990          method: 'POST',
12991          headers: {
12992            'Content-Type': 'application/json',
12993          },
12994          body: JSON.stringify({ churchId, tableName, settings }),
12995        });
12996        const data = await response.json();
12997        return data;
12998      } catch (error) {
12999        console.error('API Error saving table settings:', error);
13000        return { success: false, error: 'Network error' };
13001      }
13002    },
13003    getDefaultSettings(allColumnFields: string[]): TableSettings {
13004      return {
13005        columns: {
13006          visible: allColumnFields,
13007          order: allColumnFields
13008        },
13009        autoHideEmpty: false,
13010        defaultSort: {
13011          field: allColumnFields[0] || '',
13012          order: 'desc'
13013        }
13014      };
13015    }
13016  };
13017  EOF

14334  with open('ge_samples.json', 'r', encoding='utf-8') as f:
14335      content = f.read()
14336  # Split by the pattern ']\n\n[' to get the three arrays
14337  parts = content.split(']\n\n[')
14338  # Parse each array
14339  baptism_str = parts[0] + ']'
14340  marriage_str = '[' + parts[1] + ']'
14341  funeral_str = '[' + parts[2]
14342  baptism_records = json.loads(baptism_str)
14343  marriage_records = json.loads(marriage_str)
14344  funeral_records = json.loads(funeral_str)
14345  # Create the proper structure
14346  result = {
14347      'baptism_records': baptism_records,
14348      'marriage_records': marriage_records,
14349      'funeral_records': funeral_records
14350  }
14351  # Write back as valid JSON
14352  with open('ge_samples.json', 'w', encoding='utf-8') as f:
14353      json.dump(result, f, ensure_ascii=False, indent=2)
14354  print('File restructured successfully')
14355  "

15848  cd /var/www/orthodoxmetrics/prod && cat > /tmp/test-upload.sh << 'EOF'
15849  #!/bin/bash
15850  # Test script to login and upload image
15851  BASE_URL="http://127.0.0.1:3001"
15852  EMAIL="${1:-admin@example.com}"
15853  PASSWORD="${2:-your-password}"
15854  CHURCH_ID="${3:-46}"
15855  IMAGE_PATH="${4:-./test-image.png}"
15856  TYPE="${5:-baptism}"
15857  echo "🔐 Step 1: Logging in..."
15858  LOGIN_RESPONSE=$(curl -s -c /tmp/cookies.txt -X POST "$BASE_URL/api/auth/login" \
15859    -H "Content-Type: application/json" \
15860    -d "{\"email\":\"$EMAIL\",\"password\":\"$PASSWORD\"}")
15861  echo "Login response: $LOGIN_RESPONSE"
15862  echo ""
15863  # Extract session cookie
15864  SESSION_COOKIE=$(grep -oP 'connect\.sid\t[^\t]+' /tmp/cookies.txt | cut -f2 | head -1)
15865  if [ -z "$SESSION_COOKIE" ]; then
15866    echo "❌ Failed to get session cookie. Check credentials."
15867    exit 1
15868  fi
15869  echo "✅ Got session cookie"
15870  echo ""
15871  echo "📤 Step 2: Uploading image..."
15872  UPLOAD_RESPONSE=$(curl -s -w "\n%{http_code}" \
15873    -X POST \
15874    -H "Cookie: connect.sid=$SESSION_COOKIE" \
15875    -F "image=@$IMAGE_PATH" \
15876    -F "type=$TYPE" \
15877    "$BASE_URL/api/admin/churches/$CHURCH_ID/record-images")
15878  HTTP_CODE=$(echo "$UPLOAD_RESPONSE" | tail -n1)
15879  BODY=$(echo "$UPLOAD_RESPONSE" | sed '$d')
15880  echo "HTTP Status: $HTTP_CODE"
15881  echo "Response:"
15882  echo "$BODY" | jq '.' 2>/dev/null || echo "$BODY"

16014          # Don't intercept errors - pass them through from backend

16016          # CORS (tune/lock down as needed)
16017          add_header Access-Control-Allow-Origin $http_origin always;
16018          add_header Access-Control-Allow-Credentials true always;
16019          add_header Access-Control-Allow-Methods "GET, POST, PUT, DELETE, OPTIONS" always;

17632  cat >> /tmp/themes_routes.js << 'EOF'
17633  // GET /api/admin/churches/:id/themes - Get themes for a church
17634  router.get('/:id/themes', requireAuth, requireChurchAccess, async (req, res) => {
17635    try {
17636      const churchId = parseInt(req.params.id);
17637      // Validate church access
17638      const access = validateChurchAccess(req.user, churchId);
17639      if (!access.allowed) {
17640        return res.status(403).json(ApiResponse(false, null, {
17641          message: 'Access denied',
17642          code: 'INSUFFICIENT_PERMISSIONS',
17643          reason: access.reason
17644        }));
17645      }
17646      // Get church database name
17647      const [churches] = await getAppPool().query(
17648        'SELECT database_name FROM churches WHERE id = ? AND is_active = 1',      
17649        [churchId]
17650      );
17651      if (churches.length === 0) {
17652        return res.status(404).json(ApiResponse(false, null, {
17653          message: 'Church not found',
17654          code: 'CHURCH_NOT_FOUND'
17655        }));
17656      }
17657      // Get existing themes from the themes table
17658      const [themes] = await getAppPool().query(
17659        `SELECT themes
17660         FROM orthodoxmetrics_db.church_themes
17661         WHERE church_id = ?`,
17662        [churchId]
17663      );
17664      const themesData = themes.length > 0 && themes[0].themes ? JSON.parse(themes[0].themes) : {};
17665      res.json(ApiResponse(true, {
17666        themes: themesData
17667      }));
17668    } catch (error) {
17669      console.error('❌ Error fetching themes:', error);
17670      res.status(500).json(ApiResponse(false, null, {
17671        message: 'Failed to fetch themes',
17672        code: 'DATABASE_ERROR',
17673        details: process.env.NODE_ENV === 'development' ? error.message : undefined
17674      }));
17675    }
17676  });
17677  // POST /api/admin/churches/:id/themes - Save themes for a church
17678  router.post('/:id/themes', requireAuth, requireChurchAccess, async (req, res) => {
17679    try {
17680      const churchId = parseInt(req.params.id);
17681      const { themes } = req.body;
17682      // Validate church access
17683      const access = validateChurchAccess(req.user, churchId);
17684      if (!access.allowed) {
17685        return res.status(403).json(ApiResponse(false, null, {
17686          message: 'Access denied',
17687          code: 'INSUFFICIENT_PERMISSIONS',
17688          reason: access.reason
17689        }));
17690      }
17691      // Get church database name
17692      const [churches] = await getAppPool().query(
17693        'SELECT database_name FROM churches WHERE id = ? AND is_active = 1',      
17694        [churchId]
17695      );
17696      if (churches.length === 0) {
17697        return res.status(404).json(ApiResponse(false, null, {
17698          message: 'Church not found',
17699          code: 'CHURCH_NOT_FOUND'
17700        }));
17701      }
17702      // Create table if it doesn't exist
17703      await getAppPool().query(`
17704        CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS orthodoxmetrics_db.church_themes (     
17705          id INT AUTO_INCREMENT PRIMARY KEY,
17706          church_id INT NOT NULL,
17707          themes JSON,
17708          created_at TIMESTAMP DEFAULT CURRENT_TIMESTAMP,
17709          updated_at TIMESTAMP DEFAULT CURRENT_TIMESTAMP ON UPDATE CURRENT_TIMESTAMP,
17710          UNIQUE KEY unique_church (church_id),
17711          FOREIGN KEY (church_id) REFERENCES churches(id) ON DELETE CASCADE       
17712        ) ENGINE=InnoDB DEFAULT CHARSET=utf8mb4 COLLATE=utf8mb4_unicode_ci        
17713      `);
17714      // Upsert the themes
17715      await getAppPool().query(`
17716        INSERT INTO orthodoxmetrics_db.church_themes
17717          (church_id, themes)
17718        VALUES (?, ?)
17719        ON DUPLICATE KEY UPDATE
17720          themes = VALUES(themes),
17721          updated_at = CURRENT_TIMESTAMP
17722      `, [
17723        churchId,
17724        JSON.stringify(themes || {})
17725      ]);
17726      res.json(ApiResponse(true, {
17727        message: 'Themes saved successfully',
17728        church_id: churchId
17729      }));
17730    } catch (error) {
17731      console.error('❌ Error saving themes:', error);
17732      res.status(500).json(ApiResponse(false, null, {
17733        message: 'Failed to save themes',
17734        code: 'DATABASE_ERROR',
17735        details: process.env.NODE_ENV === 'development' ? error.message : undefined
17736      }));
17737    }
17738  });
17739  // GET /api/admin/churches/themes/global - Get global themes
17740  router.get('/themes/global', requireAuth, requireChurchAccess, async (req, res) => {
17741    try {
17742      // Get global themes from the themes table (church_id = 0 or NULL for global)
17743      const [themes] = await getAppPool().query(
17744        `SELECT themes
17745         FROM orthodoxmetrics_db.church_themes
17746         WHERE church_id IS NULL OR church_id = 0
17747         LIMIT 1`
17748      );
17749      const themesData = themes.length > 0 && themes[0].themes ? JSON.parse(themes[0].themes) : {};
17750      res.json(ApiResponse(true, {
17751        themes: themesData
17752      }));
17753    } catch (error) {
17754      console.error('❌ Error fetching global themes:', error);
17755      res.status(500).json(ApiResponse(false, null, {
17756        message: 'Failed to fetch global themes',
17757        code: 'DATABASE_ERROR',
17758        details: process.env.NODE_ENV === 'development' ? error.message : undefined
17759      }));
17760    }
17761  });
17762  // POST /api/admin/churches/themes/global - Save global themes
17763  router.post('/themes/global', requireAuth, requireChurchAccess, async (req, res) => {
17764    try {
17765      const { themes } = req.body;
17766      // Create table if it doesn't exist
17767      await getAppPool().query(`
17768        CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS orthodoxmetrics_db.church_themes (     
17769          id INT AUTO_INCREMENT PRIMARY KEY,
17770          church_id INT NULL,
17771          themes JSON,
17772          created_at TIMESTAMP DEFAULT CURRENT_TIMESTAMP,
17773          updated_at TIMESTAMP DEFAULT CURRENT_TIMESTAMP ON UPDATE CURRENT_TIMESTAMP,
17774          UNIQUE KEY unique_church (church_id),
17775          FOREIGN KEY (church_id) REFERENCES churches(id) ON DELETE CASCADE       
17776        ) ENGINE=InnoDB DEFAULT CHARSET=utf8mb4 COLLATE=utf8mb4_unicode_ci        
17777      `);
17778      // Upsert the global themes (church_id = NULL for global)
17779      await getAppPool().query(`
17780        INSERT INTO orthodoxmetrics_db.church_themes
17781          (church_id, themes)
17782        VALUES (NULL, ?)
17783        ON DUPLICATE KEY UPDATE
17784          themes = VALUES(themes),
17785          updated_at = CURRENT_TIMESTAMP
17786      `, [
17787        JSON.stringify(themes || {})
17788      ]);
17789      res.json(ApiResponse(true, {
17790        message: 'Global themes saved successfully'
17791      }));
17792    } catch (error) {
17793      console.error('❌ Error saving global themes:', error);
17794      res.status(500).json(ApiResponse(false, null, {
17795        message: 'Failed to save global themes',
17796        code: 'DATABASE_ERROR',
17797        details: process.env.NODE_ENV === 'development' ? error.message : undefined
17798      }));
17799    }
17800  });

17948        ) ENGINE=InnoDB DEFAULT CHARSET=utf8mb4 COLLATE=utf8mb4_unicode_ci        
17949      `);
17950      // Upsert the global themes (church_id = NULL for global)
17951      await getAppPool().query(`
17952        INSERT INTO orthodoxmetrics_db.church_themes
17953          (church_id, themes)
17954        VALUES (NULL, ?)
17955        ON DUPLICATE KEY UPDATE
17956          themes = VALUES(themes),
17957          updated_at = CURRENT_TIMESTAMP
17958      `, [
17959        JSON.stringify(themes || {})
17960      ]);
17961      res.json(ApiResponse(true, {
17962        message: 'Global themes saved successfully'
17963      }));
17964    } catch (error) {
17965      console.error('❌ Error saving global themes:', error);
17966      res.status(500).json(ApiResponse(false, null, {
17967        message: 'Failed to save global themes',
17968        code: 'DATABASE_ERROR',
17969        details: process.env.NODE_ENV === 'development' ? error.message : undefined
17970      }));
17971    }
17972  });
